Love Persevering

by charmed4lifekaren

Summary

AU: When Thanos snaps his fingers to end half of life in the universe Rio Vidal, Lady Death herself, uses the chaos and the power released into the universe to do the one thing she wants most; bring back the son she shared with Agatha Harkness from the Afterlife. Once she has her seven-year-old son back there is only one other thing Rio wants, Agatha, but under the influence of the Darkhold Agatha is hidden, even from Death herself.
After five years of searching Rio finally feels Agatha again, but it’s too late as the great Agatha Harkness becomes powerless, trapped under the spell of the Scarlett Witch. Not letting this be the end of their story, of their family, Death and Her son dedicate everything to working out a way to break through; watching over Agatha, never being far away even if she doesn't know them, until finally, after three years, it’s time to put their plan into motion; a plan that rests solely on Nicky's shoulders as his identity becomes a protected secret, even from Death herself.

Notes

AN: So, for a while I have been obsessed with the idea of teen actually being Nicky, rather than Billy, and that evolved into Nicky and Rio working together prior to Agatha All Along to ‘wake’ Agatha up, and then this evolved into this. I am very excited for this, have a detailed plan, hope you like what this is.
This will address the time from the snap to Agatha All Along (Will be more AU but will still have elements from at least episodes 1-5, maybe beyond that) and then the events that follow.
This chapter is on the shorter size as it sets a lot up.
I have had this chapter and the first six chapters done for a few days, but I wanted to see how 1x06 played out before posting just in case it revealed something I wanted to incorporate, which turns out I didn’t need to worry about, though I will say that the way sigils and are made in this story is a little different, and Wanda’s spell will be a little harder to reverse. I will be doing my best to update regularly but my life is pretty messy at the moment so I can’t give an exact schedule just yet.

Chapter 1

May 31 st 2018

When you’ve existed for eternity, there aren’t a lot of experiences that are new, but what Rio Vidal, also known as Lady Death, feels when A Mad Titan snaps his fingers, harnessing the power of all six infinity at once, is definitely a new experience.

As the universe unsurprisingly falls into chaos as power that hasn’t been felt since the beginning of time is released Rio realises feels something else that she has never felt before that the vale between life and death is thinner than it has ever been. Not caring about the consequences, not knowing if what she wants to do is even possible but knowing that she has to try, that she can’t pass up this opportunity, Rio puts all her focus, all her power, into one goal; getting to her son who died one hundred and fifty-five years ago.

After spending eternity delivering people to where they need to go after they died Rio has visited the vale many times, what she hasn’t done is cross over it herself. After punching through the already thin vale, making a hole big enough for her to fit through, Rio just focuses on her son, wiling to be with him, and as she travels through the realms she’s spent eons delivery people to but never visiting herself, Rio feels her strength slipping away from her, like she has the weight of everything pushing against her, trying to pull her to back to where she came from, but she doesn’t care, all she cares about is getting to her son, her Nicky, and that gives her the strength to keep going.

Having no idea how much time has passed Rio finally hears a laugh she has never forgotten, and right away she knows she is where she will find him.

“Nicky! Nicky, can you hear me!” Rio exclaims, doing her best to look around, but it’s almost like her eyes don’t work, a sensation she has never experience before.

“Mommy?” Nicky’s voice asks, and Rio sees what she thinks he is, looking just the same as when he died at seven years old, except not sick, and without a doubt Rio knows that is really him, she can feel that his soul feels the same as it did when he first came into existence. It feels like the incredible mix of her and Agatha that he is and because of that she knows, without a doubt, that he is her Nicky.

“Yeah Nicky! It’s me, I need you to come to me, Mi Conejito, follow my voice, can you do that?” Rio asks as and what feels like a couple of seconds later Rio sees him come closer to her.

“MOMMY!” Nicky yells excited, and even though neither of them have physical forms at the moment the only way Rio can describe what she feels next is the feeling of hugging her son once more.

“Oh, I’ve missed you, so much,” Rio says to her son, doing her best to ‘hold’ him close as she knows she is never going to let him go again.

“I’ve missed you too, and Mama,” Nicky says.

“Oh, we’ve missed you too, so much,” Rio says, knowing she can speak for both of them about that even though it has been a very long time since they have seen each other. “Do you want to be with us again, Nicky?” Rio asks, speaking quickly as she doesn’t know how long she has until she is forced out of this realm, all she knows is she can feel an incredible strength pushing against her, trying to force her out of this realm. “Would you like to come with me?” Rio asks, desperately hoping he will say yes, but she won’t force him, even if it breaks her not to.

“I do!” Nicky says without hesitation. “I want to be with you and Mama,” Nicky confirms.

“Then I need you to hold onto me, okay, really tight,” Rio says, having no idea if this is going to work but needing to try, knowing that this is going to be the only chance she is going to get. “No matter what, don’t let go, okay, don’t let go, no matter what, just keep holding on, don’t let go,” Rio says to her son. “Can you do that?” Rio asks.

“I can, Mommy,” Nicky says as he ‘jumps’ into her arms, and as he ‘wraps’ his legs around Rio’s waist Rio holds onto him tighter than she has ever held onto anything in her entire existence, and stops fighting the sensation trying to force her to go back. The second Rio stops fighting she can feel herself being flung backwards, and all she focuses on is holding Nicky, holding him tight, and not letting him go as they are forced out of a place Rio truly believes neither of them belong.

After being flung back the next sensation Rio feels is pain, something she hasn’t felt a whole lot of, but as she opens her eyes and looks around Rio realise two things. The first is that she is lying on her back in a field, clearly back on Earth, the second is that she isn’t alone.

“Nicky! Nicky!” Rio yells as she moves, with some difficulty, to where her son, who once again looks exactly the same as before he got sick, but is actually wearing the pyjamas he was wearing when he died. Getting to Nicky’s side Rio doesn’t hesitate for a second before she reaches out to him to her absolute relief, he is solid, he is real. “Nicky?” Rio asks, her voice breaking. “Nicky, can you open your eyes?” Rio asks and for the first time in over a hundred- and fifty-years Rio sees her son open his eyes, that are so much like hers and look at her.

“Hi Mommy,” Nicky says, smiling at her.

“Hi Mi Conejito,” Rio says, tears of joy coming to her eyes as she never thought this was possible, and she quickly pulls Nicky into her arms.

“Mommy, am I alive?” Nicky asks as he hugs his mother, not even complaining that his mother is hugging him so tightly that it almost hurts, as he understands enough to know that what just happened is amazing.

“Yeah, Nicky, yeah you are,” Rio says as she continues to hug her son, feeling, below the current chaos of the universe, that not only is her son alive, the same age he was when he died, but he is perfectly healthy too; something which means everything to Rio.

“Good,” Nicky says, as he very much wants to be alive. “Mommy? Where’s Mama?” Nicky asks, looking around and not seeing his other mother, who he also deeply missed, who he also really wants to see again.

“I don’t know,” Rio admits, as she forces herself to let go of her son so she can look at him, as seven years after Nicky died her love, her wife, Nicky’s other mother, Agatha Harkness, obtained the Darkhold, the book of the damned, and used it to hide from her; that damn book being the only thing powerful enough to hide a person from Death. “But Nicky, I promise. We’re going to find her,” Rio says, knowing that no matter what it takes she will find Agatha, she will reunite her with their son.

“Pinkie promise?” Nicky asks, looking up at his mother.

“Pinky promise,” Rio says and the two of them do just that.

“Good, I miss Mama too,” Nicky admits.

“Me too,” Rio admits, even though she has spent over a century tyring to not think about that fact, and once she does, she has to close her eyes for a second as her vision has gone blurry.

“Mommy, are you okay?” Nicky asks concerned, as he can tell that something doesn’t seem right, his mother doesn’t ‘feel’ as ‘strong’ as she always used to feel.

“Yeah, I think I’m just a little tired,” Rio tells him, but she has a nagging feeling that breaking through the vale like she just did used more of her strength than she realised. “So how about we find somewhere to stay tonight,” Rio says, being sure that with the chaos of everything that has just happened she is going to be able to find them a place.

“Okay Mommy,” Nicky says, and with some difficulty Rio manages to get to her feet, feeling a little unsteady as she does, but to her relief it passes.

Once Rio is on her feet, she takes off the thin jacket she is wearing and puts it around Nicky who has also gotten to his feet, as while it isn’t much it will give him some warmth, thankfully it’s not that cold so he should be okay.

“Do you think you can walk?” Rio asks Nicky, as considering how she feels she doesn’t think it would be a good idea to use magic to travel.

“I think so,” Nicky responds. While he doesn’t completely understand what’s been going on he knows that he had to leave his moms, that he was in a different place, and that it’s been a long time since he has to do things like walk, and even breathe.

“Okay, let me know the second you need me to carry you,” Rio tells her son, as while she isn’t completely sure she will be able to she knows that if her son needs her to she will find a way.

“I will,” Nicky promises as he reaches out and takes his mother’s hand.

As she once again feels her sons’ hand in hers, something she even let herself believe she would feel again, Rio starts to walk, each step feeling like it is taking everything in her but knowing she can’t stop until she gets Nicky to a safe place.

For almost an hour Rio and Nicky walk together, Rio not letting go of her sons hand for even a split second, as she realises that there is definitely something wrong with her, until they finally they get to a little village. Considering what she knows Thanos has just done Rio isn’t surprised to find that this little village on the Isel of Man is pretty empty.

Using that for her advantage Rio first takes Nicky to market where she collects enough food for a few days as while she doesn’t need food, though she does enjoy it especially when cooked by Agatha, Nicky does, and she knows, without a doubt, that she is always going to make sure her son has everything he needs.

Once food, as well as a few other supplies they may need, is taken care of Rio leads Nicky over to the village inn, where she breaks into a room for them, being pretty sure that no one is going to care about a little breaking and entering with everything else going on. As she wanted to make sure they would be safe Rio broke into the room in a way where she would still be able to lock the door, which is exactly what she does, as Nicky walks over to the bed.

“Mommy? What’s wrong?” Nicky asks worried as he sits on the bed, and Rio, with some difficulty, puts the food, and other supplies, down on the table, and squats down in front of him.

“Mommy’s a little tired, Mi Conejito. So, I’m going to make sure we’re safe, and then I’m going to sleep for a little while,” Rio says, knowing that when he died Nicky was too young to understand that his mommy doesn’t sleep so he won’t find anything odd about her needing to sleep. “While I’m asleep you can’t leave this room, okay? The bathroom is through there,” Rio says, pointing to it, feeling herself become weaker with every word “So use it when you need, and we have plenty of food, but you cannot leave this these rooms, and you can’t let anyone in,” Rio explains, wanting to make sure Nicky is as safe as possible as it’s what she cares about most.

“What if it’s Mama?” Nicky asks, having complete, unshakable faith, in his Mama, he truly believes that she will be able to find them, no matter what.

“If it’s Mama, let her in,” Rio says, though she very much doubts Agatha will suddenly appear, in fact, she doesn’t even know if Agatha survived Thanos’s extermination, something she is doing her best not to think about, as while she always believed, no matter what Agatha did, that she would able to feel it if Agatha as actually died, with the chaos that the universe is currently in that’s not even something she be certain off. “But no one else,” Rio explains, reaching out and pushing Nicky’s dark hair out of his face. “I need you to be brave, Sweetheart, can you do that?” Rio asks.

“I can do that, Mommy,” Nicky promises.

“Good Boy, I’m so proud of you, I love you so much,” Rio says, needing her son to know that.

“Love you too,” Nicky responds, and once he does Rio stands up, stumbling a little as she does.

Once she is standing up Rio uses the last bit of strength, she has to put up runes to keep Nicky safe, knowing that whatever is happening to her is worth it because she knows Nicky is okay, before collapsing on the bed just as the last rune is in place, her last conscious thought being, “I brought him back to us, Agatha, I finally brought him back,”

Chapter 2

As his mom collapses onto the bed Nicky is scared at first, but then he remembers the promise he made.

“I can be brave, Mommy,” Nicky assures Rio, there being a feeling deep inside of him, a feeling which he doesn’t completely understand, that tells him his mommy is going to be okay, but it’s going to take time.

Looking around the room Nicky sees a lot of things he has never seen before, and things like lights that just seem different than how he remembers. As he looks around Nicky sees something that he does know, a blanket, and pillow, remembering what his mother’s would do for him every night Nicky picks up a blanket, and a pillow which he carries over to his mother. Being gentle as he doesn’t want to hurt her Nicky gently lays the blanket over before lifting Rio’s head a little and putting the pillow underneath her, trying to make her more comfortable, not realising that a small beam of blue, that has a green and purple hue, magick goes out of him and into Rio as he does.

“That’s better,” Nicky says approvingly as he looks around. As he is sure that his mommy is as comfortable as possible Nicky starts to explore the room, making sure not to break the promise he made by leaving, and starts to inspect the things he has never seen before. As he finds everything fascinating Nicky knows that he wants to know as much as possible about this new world he has woken up in and hopes that he will get the chance to.

As he has been experiencing a timeless existence for so long Nicky doesn’t realise just how long he has been in the hotel room with his unconscious mother, all he knows he misses her. While Rio has been unconscious for three days Nicky has been learning everything he can about the room, and bathroom, he is in, and through his exploration he has found a book to read and more exciting for him he figured out how to turn on the TV, which he is watching when he realises his mommy is starting to wake up.

“Mommy?” Nicky asks, jumping down form the bed he was lying on and walking over to the bed where Rio is. “Mommy? Are you awake?” Nicky asks and to his second later Rio bolts upright, a look of fear on her face.

“Nicky!” Rio exclaims, clearly terrified for him.

“I’m right here, Mommy,” Nicky says, and the second she sees him Rio moves quickly and embraces him, needing to once again remind herself that he is alive, that everything that happened wasn’t just a dream.

“You are, you really are,” Rio says amazed, as she hugs him, kissing the top of his head. “Are you okay?” Rio asks, as she breaks apart from him, trying to figure out how long she has been unconscious for, wanting to know just how long she has left him alone.

“Yep,” Nicky says with a nod. “I’ve been watching people in the box,” Nicky says, pointing at the TV, causing Rio to smile at that description. “Is it magick, Mommy?” Nicky asks curious, as the TV reminded him of ways his mothers would bring his bedtime stories alive.

“Not exactly, it’s technology,” Rio says, before picking him up and carrying Nicky over to the bed where they both sit, Rio putting Nicky on her lap and keeping her arms around him; knowing that it feels like everything to her to have her son in her arms again.

“Nicky, what do you know about we’re you’ve been? About how long you’ve been there?” Rio asks, feeling that now she is feeling a little stronger, though she knows she is not at her full power, that this is a conversation they need to have.

“I died,” Nicky says, and while she may be death herself it does hurt Rio to hear her son talk so casually about his own death. “I wasn’t scared, I knew you made sure I was safe, there was no pain, but I missed you and Mama,” Nicky admits. “I just wanted to be with you again…. It felt wrong that I wasn’t,” Nicky admits.

“It was wrong,” Rio confirms, as while she knew that it was her sons time when he died, that he needed to move on, that didn’t prevent it from feeling completely wrong, a feeling which she knows Agatha agreed with.

“I’ve been gone a long time,” Nicky says, knowing that, though he couldn’t tell how long.

“You have, too long,” Rio says, kissing the top of his head. “While you’ve been gone a lot has changed,” Rio admits, trying to think of the best way to explain. “One of the things that have changed is that people have invented amazing things, things that are almost like magick,” Rio explains, that being the best explanation she can think to give.

“Wow,” Nicky says amazed. “Do witches still have to hide?” Nicky asks curious, as he remembers both his mothers always teaching him about making sure he was careful who he used his magick around.

“We do,” Rio confirms, knowing that while Superheroes have become common witches still remain mostly hidden, something which is probably a good thing. “Nicky, do you remember what Mama was teaching you about how to use your magick?” Rio asks, as she knows that Nicky was just starting to come into his powers before, he got sick, and that Agatha was starting to teach him as their magicks were similar, that their magicks connected them in a way Rio didn’t completely understand, and that Agatha wanted to make sure he truly understood it. She wanted to make sure he never felt the shame or self-hate her mother made her feel.

“A little,” Nicky admits, then he gets a sheepish look on his face. “The bathroom was really dark, so I used magick to make it light,” Nicky admits, feeling worried that he did something wrong.

“Oh Mi Conejito, that’s okay, you did nothing wrong,” Rio assures him.

“When we find Mama will she teach me magick again?” Nicky asks curious, and Rio can tell that he wants that.

“I’m sure she will,” Rio says, believing that, though she hopes that whatever lessons Agatha gives don’t include the Darkhold as she doesn’t want that damn book anywhere near their son. “But until we find her how about you and I work together to see just what you can do?” Rio asks, as she knows that she needs to make sure Nicky has at least some control over his magick, that it’s too dangerous for both of them for him not to, and for a moment Nicky looks hesitant, as magick is always something he shared more with his Mama than his Mom, but he gives a small nod.

“Okay,” Nicky says.

“It will just be until we find Mama, and then you can get back to your lessons together,” Rio assures her son, as she can see his hesitance, something she doesn’t take personally as she saw the way magick connected Agatha and Nicky; something which not only amazed to witness, but which she considered a privilege to see.

“I like learning from you too, Mommy, I just know that I’m meant to learn magick with, and from, Mama,” Nicky explains, and Rio would bet that he doesn’t understand everything he is saying, even though he is certain of what he is saying.

“Oh Sweetheart, I know, it’s okay,” Rio assures him. “When we find Mama, she is going to be so happy to teach you again, to be with you again,” Rio assures Nicky, knowing that without a doubt.

“I’m going to be happy too,” Nicky responds. “How long do you think until we find her?” Nicky asks.

“I don’t know,” Rio admits, as she knows that she can’t predict anything because of the damn Darkhold. “But I know we’re not going to give up until we find her,” Rio says, knowing that she doesn’t care how long it takes, she just hopes it doesn’t take too long as she doesn’t want Agatha to miss too much of their sons second chance.

“Mama would never give up on us,” Nicky says in a matter of fact tone of voice. “We can’t give up on her,”

“We won’t, Mi Conejito, no matter what, I promise,” Rio assures her son as the two of them drift into silence as they sit together, Rio having no idea where to start the search for Agatha but knowing that she isn’t going to give up until they find her, while Nicky is just glad to be alive again.

For over two weeks Rio and Nicky have stayed in at the Inn they broke into the Isle of Man, doing so for three reasons; the first is that Rio needed time to heal, the second is Rio wanted to slowly introduce Nicky to the new world not wanting him to become overwhelmed, and the third, a reason she didn’t even tell Nicky, is that a part of Rio was hoping that Agatha would feel such a surge of magick that she would come to investigate.

As two weeks passed with no sign of Agatha Rio knew it was time for them to move on and start their search. While Rio knows she doesn’t have all her strength back, she does know that she is strong enough to travel. Once they get back to the mainland Rio debates where to start the search and as she feels a familiar tug which tells her she is needed to do her job.

Knowing she can’t take Nicky with her Rio brings them to a place that she and Agatha once considered their sanctuary, their safe place, as while she suspects it would be the last place Agatha would go to it is a place where Rio knows Nicky would be safe, which is what she needs right now.

“Mommy, what is this place?” Nicky asks as Rio leads him into a small cottage hidden in an English forest, one that she has checked in on ever few months to make sure was not just still standing, but still safe.

“My first home,” Rio says, as in her entire existence this was the first place that felt like a home to her.

“You lived here with Mama,” Nicky realises, as he looks around at the small living area.

“You can tell that?” Rio asks curious, wondering just what he is sensing, and Nicky nods.

“You and Mama lived here…. a long time ago… you were happy,” Nicky realises, not feeling completely sure how he knows that, but knowing that.

“Yeah, we were,” Rio confirms. “We lived here after we got married,” Rio explains, as after they met, after Agatha got freedom from her mother, she and Agatha spent fifty years exploring the world together, causing chaos, before getting married.

“I love that story,” Nicky says with a smile, as the story of how his parents got married is one of his favourite stories ever.

“Me too,” Rio admits, and as she does, she finds herself being swept back into her memory.

1754 – England.

Surrounded by darkness Rio and Agatha, side by side, made their way in since towards small lights in the distance. After walking for about a minute Rio and Agatha walked into a clearing where there were several lit touches waiting for them.

“You did all this?” Agatha asked, as she looked around, seeing that the entire clearing was covered in flowers as well as well as torches to make it bright.

“I wanted it to be special,” Rio said, as she led Agatha to the centre of the clearing, where there is a specific circle having been made out of flowers.

“It’s amazing,” Agatha said amazed, as before meeting Rio she never had someone who would do something so incredible for her. “I love you,” Agatha said to Rio.

“I love you too,” Rio said as she reached out and put pushed Agatha’s hair out of her face. “Mi Amour? What’s wrong?” Rio asked, as she saw hesitance behind Agatha’s eyes.

“Are you sure you want this?” Agatha asked hesitantly. “Sure, you want me?” Agatha asked in a quite voice.

“I’ve never been more sure of anything in my entire existence,” Rio told Agatha. “You are the most incredible person I have ever met, you are my heart, my soul, my everything, and I want to make it official,” Rio told Agatha.

“That’s what I want too,” Agatha said. “I just never thought I deserved something like this, never thought I deserved to be loved,” Agatha said, all the hateful words her mother said over her lifetime replaying clearly in her mind, even though it has been half a century since she died.

“You do,” Rio said, before leaning forward and kissing Agatha, giving her a gentle, tender kiss rather than one that is as passionate as they usually exchanged. “And I’m going to spend the rest of eternity making you believe that,” Rio said, and once she did she realised something. “Midnight, on a full moon, it’s time,” Rio said to Agatha.

“It is,” Agatha confirmed. “Let’s do this,” Agatha said, and the two of them took a step back from each other.

Once they both took a step back from each other Rio and Agatha both clasped hands, and perform a ritual the spent a year researching, one that bound them both magically and spiritually, forever, one that essentially married them in every way that mattered.

“Mommy?” Nicky asks, as his mother has been staring out to space. “Mommy? Are you okay?” Nicky asks concerned.

“Yeah, Mi Conejito, I’m okay,” Rio says, as she shakes off memories of her past, something which is difficult considering where they are. As she does her best to shake off memories she feels a stronger tug which tells her she has to go do her job, which means she has to talk to Nicky as for the last couple of weeks she has been going to do her job while he has been sleeping and making sure she is back before he wakes, but she knows she can’t hide that from him any longer. “Let’s sit down,” Rio says, leading Nicky over to the couch and the two of them sit down. “Nicky, do you remember when I would sometimes have to go away to do my job?” Rio asks as being death herself she doesn’t have handle everything alone, she can delegate certain things, even if she has to handle most things herself.

“Are you leaving me, Mommy?” Nicky asks, becoming upset.

“Not for long,” Rio admits, hitting that she is hurting her son, but she has no choice. “My job is very important and there are things that only I can do so I have to go, but I won’t be gone for long, and I promise, I will come back,” Rio assures Nicky, it feeling wrong to leave her son alone, but when she doesn’t know where Agatha is she has no other option as there is not a single other being in the universe that she would trust with their son.

“Pinkie promise?” Nicky asks.

“Pinkie promise,” Rio says, and the two of them do a pinkie promise. “While I’m gone, you’re going to stay here, and I’ll make sure you’re safe, but you can’t leave, okay? You have to stay inside,” Rio says, as she knows it’s the only way to keep him safe is if he is inside a structure she can secure, a structure she can hide from everyone. “Can you do that for me?” Rio asks.

“I can Mommy,” Nicky assures her.

“Good,” Rio says relieved, feeling another tug. “Do you want to look around the cottage?” Rio asks, as she wants to make sure Nicky is comfortable before she goes.

“Sure,” Nicky responds, and Rio proceeds to show him around, making sure he knows where everything he is going to need, including the bed that is his, is.

“I’ll be back as soon as I can,” Rio promises Nicky, giving him a hug and a kiss on his head. “I love you,” Rio tells her son.

“I love you too,” Nicky responds, and when he and Rio break apart Rio reluctantly walks away from her son, leaving him behind but doing everything in her power to make sure he is safe; something which makes her feel comforted because she knows Nicky would be safe, but which does nothing to lessen her guilt she is feeling.

A few hours after Rio walked away from Nicky, she lowers the protection of the cottage before walking back in. As she walks into the cottage Rio is surprised to find Nicky fast asleep on the couch rather than in his own bed like she was expecting.

“You were waiting for me,” Rio realises, being able to remember when Agatha would do the same, on the same couch. For a few moments Rio watches her son sleep, memorizing everything about him, taking comfort in the fact that she can see him breathing, before walking over to him. “Let’s get you more comfortable,” Rio says as she gently picks up her son, and carries him into his room.

Once in Nicky’s room Rio gently lays Nicky down on the bed, tucks him in and places a gentle kiss on his head. “I’ve missed you so much,” Rio says to her son, before sitting down next to him, planning on watching him until morning to make sure he is okay.

Chapter 3

August 9 th 2018

Just over two months have passed since Rio managed to pull of a miracle and bring her son back to life and ever since the two of them have been obsessively searching for Agatha. Between wanting to make sure Nicky was safe and protected, and wanting to slowly introduce Nicky to the new world, so that he is not overwhelmed, Rio has been moving them very frequently, though she knows the cottage will be there for when they want to stay in one place for a little longer.

For the last two months Rio has been using the times where Nicky has been sleeping to do one of two things either her job, as doesn’t want to leave him alone when he is awake for too long, or obsessively researching, tyring to find anything that could be Agatha, or lead them to her, but as, Nicky sleeps on a sunny Thursday morning Rio isn’t doing either of those things, she is doing something which to her is much more important. Just like she has been all night Rio is in the kitchen, of the current house they are squatting in, putting the finishing touches on something she has been working on all night.

“Done,” Rio says proudly as she places the last candle on a, rather lopsided, birthday cake, before lighting all eight of them. “I think he’s going to like it,” Rio says, knowing that she could have done a better job if she used magick, but making a birthday cake for Nicky is something she wanted to do from scratch, without magick.

Picking up the cake, and the present she has spent weeks tracking down, Rio heads into the, very comfortable bedroom, Nicky is sleeping in, knowing that thanks to the Snap it is easy to find abandoned houses in very good condition something which she has been using to her advantage.

“Nicky, wake up, Mi Conejito,” Rio says as she walks into the room, turning the light on she does.

“Mommy?” Nicky asks, then she notices what she is holding. “It’s my birthday,” Nicky realises, smiling at that.

“It is,” Rio confirms as she walks over to him. “Do you remember what that means?” Rio asks.

“It means I get to make a wish,” Nicky says excitedly.

“Yep, and you get presents too,” Rio tells her son, lowering the cake so that it is closer to him. “Happy birthday Nicky,” Rio tells her son. “Make a wish,” Rio says, and getting a look of complete concentration on his face Nicky blows out all eight candles in one go. “One go, good job!” Rio tells her son. “So,” Rio says, as she puts the cake on the bedside table, but keeps hold of the present she is holding, and sits down next to him. “Do you want to tell me what you wished for?” Rio asks curious.

“Mama,” Nicky says, and Rio has to fight back tears at that, as her heart breaks for her son. “I wished for Mama to be here… that’s what I want most,” Nicky admits, as he looks up at Rio.

“It’s what I want most too, and Nicky I’m really sorry we haven’t found her yet,” Rio says, once again finding herself cursing the Darkhold as she knows that if it wasn’t for that damn book she would have been able to reunite Nicky with his other mother by now, which is what she knows Agatha wants more than anything, but she can’t help but feel like she is letting her son down by not having already done so. “But we’re going to keep trying, we’re not going to give up,” Rio assures Nicky.

“I know,” Nicky responds, believing that, but it is also clear that he is sad about not seeing his mother.

“I know it’s not the same as Mama being here, but I have something of hers, something I wanted to give you,” Rio says, giving the present she is holding to Nicky. “Open it,” Rio says encouragingly, and Nicky opens the present to reveal a very old book.

“It’s a book,” Nicky says, but even he can tell that it is more than that.

“It is, but it’s more than that,” Rio explains, confirming what Nicky has already realised. “Mama has always wanted to learn everything she could about magick, she always wants to learn more, understand more, always wants to expand her knowledge,” Rio explains, knowing that Agatha would often say that knowledge can be more powerful than raw power, and one of the things she loved most was watching Agatha study. “Long before you were born, she started to write her own spell book so she could keep a record of her knowledge,” Rio explains, knowing that that particular book doesn’t have anything too dangerous in it as she checked. “She gave it to me for safekeeping, but I know it’s always meant to be yours,” Rio explains to her son.

“Mama wrote this whole book?” Nicky asks amazed.

“She did,” Rio says, knowing it’s not the only book of magick Agatha has written but it’s not the time for that conversation.

“Wow,” Nicky says amazed, as he starts to flicker through the pages, finding it fascinating, looking so much like Agatha as he does, and together Nicky and Rio celebrate Nicky’s eight birthday by eating birthday cake in bed while Nicky reads the book that makes him feel a little closer to his mama; but while they do have a good time it is clear that they both feel Agatha’s absence.

October 2018

Another two months have passed since Nicky’s eighth birthday and ever he and Rio have continued to look for Agatha. As she heard some talk of a magick user causing chaos in the Scottish Highlands Rio has taken Nicky there, but to her disappointment it quickly became clear that it wasn’t Agatha behind the chaos.

Returning to the current house she and Nicky have been squatting in, having been gone longer than she would like, Rio is surprised to find all the windows open, something which worries her as she knows it’s quiet cold.

“Nicky?” Rio calls worried s she walks in. “Nicky where are you?” Rio asks, as she looks around the main living area of the house they are staying in, and as she does, she sees Nicky huddled in the corner, clearly shivering. “NICKY!” Rio yells in terror as she runs to her son, feeling the most awful sense of déjà vu, as she throws herself down in front of him. “Nicky? Nicky? what happened, Mi Conjito?” Rio asks as she reaches out and touches her realising that he is cold to the touch.

“I wanted …. Some…fresh air… so I opened the window…. I couldn’t close it,” Nicky admits. “I’m sorry… I… couldn’t remember…. How to make…. Make a fire,” Nicky says as he continues to shiver, Rio feeling incredibly guilty about being gone for so long, as she knows this wouldn’t have happened if she was around.

“Oh Sweetheart, it’s okay, you have nothing to apologize for,” Rio says, as she pulls a blanket of the couch and using it to wrap around Nicky. “We’re going to get you warm, and we’re going to get you help, okay, you’re going to be okay,” Rio tells her son, her abilities as death telling her that her son isn’t currently dying but that he is very sick, which means she has only a small window of time. “Come on, Sweetheart, I’ve got you,” Rio says, gathering Nicky into her arms, holding the blanket around him, trying to keep him as warm, and close, as possible, before running, feeling glad that there is a car in the garage because it means she can drive him to the hospital, knowing that he is too weak to teleport him or travel by any other magical means.

Knowing that she broke every single road law that exists, and not caring at all, Rio finally gets to the nearest hospital. Not caring that she is stopped in the ambulance parking Rio ignores everyone trying to talk to her, trying to stop her, and just picks up her son, and carries him into the emergency room.

“Help! I need help!” Rio asks, her voice full of panic, as she carries Nicky into the emergency room, hating that they are in such an uncontrolled environment, but knowing that when it comes to saving someone’s life doctors can do more than she can.

“What happened?” A nurse asks, coming out from beneath the desk.

“I got home, and all the windows were open, he’s so cold, I don’t know how long he has been like this,” Rio explains, guilt rising up inside of her as she knows that if he dies, again, it will be her fault.

“Okay, follow me,” The nurse says, leading Rio to a bed. “What’s his name? how old is he?” The nurse asks.

“Nicky… Nicholas Scratch,” Rio says, saying the fake name she and Agatha decided on when Nicky was born as a way to protect him from their enemies without even thinking about even though the name they both considered to be his true name is Nicholas Vidal-Harkness. “He’s eight,” Rio answers as she puts Nicky down on the bed.

“Any medical conditions? Or past medical issues?” The nurse asks.

“Pneumonia,” Rio says, her voice breaking, as while it wasn’t called that a hundred and fifty-five years ago that’s what killed her son. “Last year… It was bad,” Rio explains, stretching the truth a little, but from the point of view of Nicky’s body that’s when he had pneumonia. “Please, please help him,” Rio begs.

“We will, ma’am,” The nurse says, as several doctors come running over to the bed. “But we need you to give us some space so we can work,” The nurse says.

“No, I’m not leaving my son,” Rio says, and one of the doctors walk over to her, as there is no way she is going to leave her son when he is so sick.

“Ma’am, we will do everything we can to help your son, we will give him our very best care, but we need you out of the room to do it,” The Doctor tells Rio, who looks over at Nicky.

“You have to save him,” Rio threatens, though from the doctor’s perspective she just sounds like a desperate mother, which she is.

“We will do everything we can,” The doctor says, and two security guards practically drag Rio into the waiting room,

“Nicky! I’m right here! I’m not going anywhere! I love you!” Rio yells to her son, as the security guards stand in front of the door.

“You’ll have to wait out here ma’am, the doctors will be out to talk to you when they can,” The security guard tells Rio, making it clear that they aren’t going to let her past as Rio realises that forcing her way past them will just mean she won’t be able to be with Nicky.

“Damn it,” Rio says angrily, and she proceeds to walk over to the nearest wall which she punches as hard as she can. “Damn it Agatha, you should be here,” Rio says as she punches the wall again. “Why didn’t you have to become so obsessed with that damn book, why did you have to hide yourself,” Rio says, her voice breaking feeling both angry and devastated, knowing that this cannot be how Nicky’s second chance ends, and finding it easier to feel the anger at Agatha hiding herself rather than the guilt she feels for leaving Nicky alone. “We need you,” Rio mutters as she slides down the wall and breaks down into tears, having no idea what she is going to do if Nicky dies again.

Having no idea how long she has been waiting but knowing that she has ignored several ‘tugs’ that tells her she needs to do her job, Rio just sits on the ground, staring at the doors that lead into the ER until finally she sees the doors open and the doctors from earlier walk out.

“Mrs Scratch,” The Doctor says, walking over to her.

“How is he?” Rio asks, not bothering to correct the doctor about her name, as while she can tell that he is alive, which means everything to her, she can’t tell more than that.

“He’s stable,” The doctor answers. “He does have pneumonia again, and because of that we would like to admit him so that he can receive IV antibiotics,” The Doctor explains, Rio knowing that antibiotics is something that wasn’t an option last time.

“Doctor, is he going to be okay?” Rio asks, as she doesn’t care about anything other than that.

“I believe so,” The Doctor says. “We are only admitting him because he’s had pneumonia fairly recently, but from his test results, including the chest x-ray, I am confident that he will be able to go home in a few days,” The Doctor explains, causing Rio to feel unbelievably relieved.

“Thank you,” Rio says relieved. “Can I see him?” Rio asks as nothing is going to stop her, but she thought it would be best to ask first.

“Of course, nurse Athena will show you the way,” The Doctor says, and to Rio’s relief she is shown right through to where her son is.

“Hi, hi Nicky,” Rio says, bending down and kissing his head, being pretty sure her healing ability won’t help because it didn’t help last time, but still trying, before sitting down next to him, taking his hand as she does. “You’re going to be okay, Mi Conejito and we’re going to find Mama, and everything’s going to be okay, I promise,” Rio says to her son, as she moves his hair out his face. “But you need to stay with me, okay? We can only find Mama together,” Rio says, and she just sits by Nicky and watches as he breathes, becoming hypnotised by his son’s chest rising and falling, her magick telling her that he is not out of the woods yet; which tells her she is not moving away from her sons side, no matter what the doctors say or do.

Three days have passed since Rio’s rushed Nicky to hospital and since being allowed to sit next to him she hasn’t left his side since, ignoring everything else, including her job. As both the doctors, and Rio’s magicks, say that Nicky is going to be okay he has been released from hospital.

Because she didn’t want to risk being far away from the hospital in case something else happens Rio has broken into another house closer to the hospital which is where she and Nicky are going to be staying, at least for a little while.

“Are you okay? How’s your chest feeling?” Rio asks as she helps Nicky into the bed.

“I’m okay, Mommy,” Nicky assures his mother, as she tucks him in. “I feel much better,” Nicky assures her.

“Good, that’s really good,” Rio says, fighting back her reaction as she doesn’t want to scare Nicky.

“Mommy, were you scared?” Nicky asks curious, and Rio debates the best way to answer that.

“Yeah, I was,” Rio admits, as she moves and sits down next to him, feeling that if she wants Nicky to be honest with her then she should be honest with him. “Where you?” Rio asks curious, as she puts her arm around her son.

“I was,” Nicky admits. “I knew that you would do everything to help me, but I was scared,” Nicky admits. “I don’t want to leave you or Mama again,” Nicky admits, as he snuggles into Rio’s side.

“I don’t want that either,” Rio admits, kissing the top of his head. “Nicky we’re going to find Mama, and we’re going to be together, the three of us, just like it always should have been,” Rio promises. “I love you so much,” Rio says to her son.

“I love you too,” Nicky responds. “Mommy, can you tell me a story?” Nicky asks.

“Of course,” Rio assures him. “How about the story of how Mama and I made it so we could have you?” Rio asks, knowing she will have to leave out of some of the details.

“Sure,” Nicky says interested, and Rio proceeds to tell her son the story of the Witches Road, and the lengths she and Agatha went to to make it so they were able to have a child that was biologically both of these.

December 2018

Two months have passed since Nicky got sick and to Rio’s absolute relief Nicky is doing a lot better. Because she couldn’t bare something like that happening again, Rio has made sure that every time she has to leave Nicky, she goes over how to make a fire, both with and without magick, and a few other basic skills to do her best to make sure he is okay when she can’t be with him.

As she realised that Christmas is coming, something which she usually ignores, Rio decided she wanted to make it special for Nicky and because of that she has brought him to London after their latest lead on Agatha turned out to be a dead end.

“Everything’s so… tall,” Nicky says shocked, looking around at all the tall buildings, as he and Rio walk down the straight together, Rio holding her son’s hand.

“Yeah, it is,” Rio tells her son. “We can go back to the country if this is too much,” Rio says, as they weave their way through the people together.

“No, it’s….” Nicky starts to say, then he freezes.

“Nicky? What’s wrong?” Rio ask concerned, as she has never seen him freeze like that.

“That lady is going to die,” Nicky says, sounding certain of that fact.

“What lady?” Rio asks, trying to figure out what is going on, what her son has realised, but before Nicky can answer her question, they both hear a car honk and an awful crash, seconds later Rio feels a tug which tells her the woman is dead.

“You have to help her move on,” Nicky says to his mother.

“I do,” Rio says looking around for somewhere safe for Nicky to go “Can you wait at the café while I do that?” Rio asks her son, noticing a café right by them, who nods. “I’ll be right back,” Rio tells her son. “Okay, it will be seconds to you,” Rio explains, as while it will be longer for her it won’t be for Nicky.

“I’ll be okay, Mommy,” Nicky assures his mother, before walking over to café, knowing that his mother needs to do her job, while Rio is focusing on doing her job so that she can get back to her son, knowing there is a very intense conversation they need to have.

A couple of hours after Nicky accurately predicted that someone was going to die, he and Rio are arriving back at the most recent house they are squatting in.

“Mommy can I go read my book before diner?” Nicky asks curious.

“Not right now, there’s something we need to talk about,” Rio says as she leads Nicky over to the couch.

“You want to talk about what happened in the street,” Nicky realises.

“I do,” Rio confirms. “Nicky, how did you know that woman was going to die?” Rio asks, wanting to understand better what is going on with her son as while she and Agatha talked hypothetically about what ‘abilities’ Nicky could have inherited from her the reality is very different.

“I just knew,” Nicky says with a shrug, not being able to explain how he knew as he just knew. “She bumped my arm, and I just knew that she was going to die, that there was nothing that could have saved her,” Nicky explains, and Rio feels relieved that it seems that the ability is at least triggered by touch which likely means they are going to be able to control it.

“Have you ever experienced something like that before?” Rio asks curious, trying to make sense of everything, and Nicky nods.

“A few weeks ago, a bird flew into the house, I tried to pick it up and I just knew it was going to die, no matter what I did,” Nicky says, his voice breaking. “And it did Mommy,” Nicky says, tears coming to his eyes.

“Oh Sweetheart,” Rio says, leaning forward and embracing her son. “I’m sorry you’re experiencing this,” Rio admits, knowing it’s her fault, and feeling worried about the kind of effect this is going to have on Nicky as he grows up as she can’t imagine it’s a burden easy for him to carry.

“Why am I?” Nicky asks. “It feels different to my magick,” Nicky admits, as for him it feels like he has two ‘different’ sources of magick in him that feel different from each other.

“That’s because it is… in some ways,” Rio admits, as the two of them break apart so Rio can look at him. “Nicky, you know who I am,” Rio says, very much wishing Agatha was by her side for this conversation.

“Of course, you’re Mommy,” Nicky says, like that is obvious, and Rio has to smile at that, knowing that when it came to Nicky, and Agatha too, they see her as herself, as Rio, first, not the cosmic being she is.

“I am,” Rio confirms. “But I’m also more than that,” Rio admits. “You know that, right?” Rio asks her son.

“I do,” Nicky confirms. “You’re death,” Nicky says.

“I am,” Rio confirms. “And because you’re my son I think, just like you got magick from Mama, you’re getting some abilities from me too,” Rio tells her son, though she has no idea just what he is going to get from her. “Nicky, I’m going to be honest with you, I don’t know exactly what it means for you being my son,” Rio admits, knowing it was the exact kind of thing Agatha would research, not her. “I don’t know what you’re going to be able to do because of that, but what I do know is that we’ll figure it out together,” Rio promises. “You’re not alone Nicky, we’ll figure this out,” Rio assures her son, and while Nicky nods Rio notices something about the look on her face. “What is it, Mi Conejito? You can ask me anything, no matter what, always,” Rio assures her son.

“Mommy is Mama dead?” Nicky asks, and it breaks Rio’s heart to even hear him asking that question.

“No,” Rio assures her son, as while she wasn’t certain when the snap first happened, she is sure of that now. “Nicky, Mama’s alive, I know that without a doubt,” Rio assures him.

“Then why can’t we find her?” Nicky asks, and even though Rio has been expecting the question for months she knows preparing for it isn’t going to be any easier to answer.

“Because Mama is hiding herself from me,” Rio explains.

“Why? Why would Mama do that?” Nicky asks confused, as in his memories he only remembers his mothers loving each other, wanting to be with each other.

“A long time ago we had a fight, a really bad fight,” Rio admits, choosing her words carefully because she doesn’t want to risk Nicky realising that their fight was about his death because she doesn’t want him to blame himself, because she is the only one to blame “Mama was really angry, and upset, and because of that she made sure I couldn’t find her in the way I could find anyone else,” Rio admits. “But Nicky you need to know it’s me Mama is mad at, it’s me she doesn’t want to see, not you, never you,” Rio assures her son. “And I know, without a shadow of a doubt, that if Mama knew you were with me, she would make it so we could find her in a second,” Rio assures Nicky.

“I really miss her,” Nicky admits.

“I miss her too,” Rio admits, and as she does, she gets an idea. “I have something for you, I was going to give it to you at Christmas, but I think you need it now,” Rio tells her son. “I’ll be right back,” Rio says, getting up, leaving her son feeling curious, and a few moments later she returns with a wrapped present, which she gives to Nicky. “I know this doesn’t make up for Mama not being here, and I am so sorry because it’s my fault,” Rio says, knowing that.  “But I thought you’d like this,” Rio reveals, and Nicky opens the gift to reveal a framed picture of Agatha, something which it took Rio months to track down as it turns out that while Agatha has been in a lot of pictures of her over the years there were very few where she was in the foreground rather than in the background, and even less that Rio considered good enough to give to their son.

“It’s Mama,” Nicky says amazed, reaching up and touching the image, feeling that she looks just like she did when he last saw her.

“It is,” Rio confirms. “It’s not the same, but I thought that this way it would almost be like you could have Mama with you,” Rio tells her son, who hugs her in response.

“Thank you,” Nicky says to his mother, the gift meaning everything to him. “Mommy?” Nicky asks hesitantly, without moving out of his moms arms.

“Yeah Sweetheart?” Nicky asks.

“How are we going to find Mama if she’s hidden from you?” Nicky asks curious.

“By not giving up, and sticking together,” Rio assures her son, as she feels him nod against her, and Rio just continues to hug her son, feeling overwhelmed, guilty, and how much she loves her son all at the same time.

Chapter 4

Chapter 4

AN: Thank you so much for such an incredible response to this story, it means everything to me. Please let me know what you think.

February 2019

Two months have passed since Nicky accurately predicted that someone was going to die, and while he hasn’t had any other moments like that, partly because Rio has been keeping them in secluded locations, away from other people, both Rio and Nicky are working on trying to figure out just what he inherited from his mother who happens to be Death.

As they have once again hit a dead end trying to find Agatha Rio, who could tell that Nicky was very disappointed, decided that she needs to do something to cheer her son up and after a lot of thinking she decided that the best way to do that is to take Nicky to one of the places where created a memory with Agatha that she still treasures.

“Mommy, what are we doing here?” Nicky asks curious, as Rio has brough them to a frozen lake in the middle of nowhere.

“I thought we could go ice skating,” Rio reveals. “A really long time ago Mama and I came here, we were camping long time, keeping warm by magick,” Rio says, smiling slightly as she remembers back fondly, but she knows that the specific thing she is remembering isn’t something she will be sharing with her son anytime soon. “Then at midnight, under a full moon, we went ice skating, here,” Rio reveals. “We had the most incredible time,” Rio admits. “So, I was thinking, we could go ice skating together, what do you think?” Rio asks curious.

“I’d like that,” Nicky responds, smiling as he likes doing thinks that make him feel close to both his mothers.

“Great,” Rio and she uses magick to change the shoes they are both wearing into skates. “You ready?” Rio asks her son, who nods. “Then come on,” Rio says, as she takes her son’s hand, and leads him over to the ice.

Once on the ice Rio and Nicky start to skate together, Nicky being nervous at first, but he quickly relaxes, and they both end up having an amazing time together.

“Mommy, I want to try skating on my own,” Nicky says to her. “Can I?” Nicky asks.

“Of course, Mi Conejito,” Rio says, and she lets go of Nicky’s hand, allowing him to skate off on his own.

For a few minutes Rio watches as a hawk as Nicky skates around, looking beyond thrilled, and as he does Rio can imagine, just for a second, that Agatha is with them. She can imagine that the three of them are having an amazing moment together, as a family, rather than it being something else Agatha is missing out on because of her.

March 2019

About a month has passed since Rio took Nicky skating and ever since they have continued their search for Agatha while also trying to figure out exactly what Nicky inherited from Rio. It’s the early hours of the morning and while Nicky is soundly asleep in his bed in the latest house, they are squatting in Rio isn’t, and not just because she doesn’t really need to sleep.

Sneaking into the room Nicky is in Rio realises that he must have fell asleep reading Agatha’s spell book, something which doesn’t surprise her, because it is open on the bed next to her. being as quiet as possible Rio checks to make sure he is sleeping soundly, which he is. After making sure Nicky is asleep, and peaceful Rio picks up the spell book, closes it, and puts it on the bedside table.

As she puts down the book Rio sees what else is there, the picture of Agatha, after glancing at Nicky, and once again checking to make sure he is asleep, Rio picks up the photo.

“I miss you,” Rio says to the picture, keeping her voice low so that she doesn’t wake Nicky. “Where are you today?” Rio asks, as she knows that Agatha will be in pain today as it’s the anniversary of when Nicky died. “Are you okay? Are you lost in the Darkhold?” Rio asks, as that terrifies her the possibility that Agatha is so corrupted, so lost, in the Darkhold that they will never be able to reach her. “I know you hate me, and if it meant finding you, I’d deal with that,” Rio admits. “I just want to see you again, want you to know Nicky,” Rio admits, reaching up and wiping a tear away, as she stares at the picture.

For a little while Rio stares at the picture of the women she loves before putting it down. After putting the picture down Rio walks over to an armchair that is in the corner of the room, where she sits down. Sitting in the chair Rio’s complete attention is on her son as she spends the rest of the night watching him sleep, knowing that with it being the anniversary of his death she needs to spend all night making sure he is okay.

June 1 st 2019

Less than three months have passed since the anniversary of when Nicky died and as Rio wanted to give them a chance to breathe, to spend some time being able to figure out what their next move is going to be, where they are going to search next without making it so they have to move every few days Rio once again brought Nicky to the cottage she considers to be her first home where they have been staying for several weeks.

As it is about time for lunch Rio is walking outside the cottage where she sees Nicky clearly practicing with his magick as he is holding the spell book in one hand, is muttering in Latin, and his blue magick is clearly dancing around his other hand.

“Nicky?” Rio asks, trying to get his attention before walking over to him so that she doesn’t actually surprise him, and Nicky turns to look at her. “What are you trying to do?” Rio asks curious.

“I’m trying to transmute plastic into flowers,” Nicky reveals, as he closes the book and sits down on the ground. “It’s not working,” Nicky says, feeling annoyed, as Rio walks over to him, noticing the frustrated look on her son’s face.

“Transmuting can be hard, you just need to practice,” Rio says as she sits down on the ground with Nicky.

“I just don’t understand,” Nicky says, feeling disappointed in himself.

“Don’t understand what, Sweetheart?” Rio asks her son.

“How I can blast, and move things, easily, but can’t do a spell that Mama described as simple,” Nicky says, feeling frustrated at his progress, and just like she does a hundred times a day Rio wishes that Agatha wasn’t hidden away beneath the Darkholds influence and was instead with them.

“It’s different types of magick,” Rio says, trying to think of what Agatha would say if she were present, though she also knows the difficulty Agatha had with her magick when she was a child, so she doesn’t want that for Nicky. “Nicky, for a witch you’re still incredibly young, your magick is still developing,” Rio explains. “You’re powerful already because of what you inherited from Mama and I, but you’ve still got a long way to go,” Rio explains. “I don’t know what you’re going to be able to do when you’ve fully come into your powers, but I know that you can’t beat yourself up for not being able to do something when you’re still learning,” Rio explains.

“So, you don’t think Mama would be disappointed that I couldn’t do the spell?” Nicky asks sheepishly as he looks down at the ground, as he knows he never wants to disappoint his Mama.

“Of course not,” Rio assures him. “Your Mama would never be disappointed in you,” Rio tells her son, stressing the never, Nicky nods, as he starts to play with the grass.

While Nicky starts to play with the grass Rio can tell that he wants to say something else, but she can also tell that he isn’t quite ready and because of that she just watches, giving him silent support as she resists the urge to make a flower appear as she isn’t sure that will help with what he is currently feeling.

“It’s been a year,” Nicky finally says, several minutes later.

“I know,” Rio says, knowing that he is talking about the fact that it has been a year since she brought him back to life.

“I thought we would have found Mama by now,” Nicky admits, and Rio feels a rush of guilt at that.

“Nicky, I’m really sorry we haven’t,” Rio tells him, having no idea what else to say to that.

“I know you are, it’s not your fault Mommy,” Nicky assures his mother. “I just really want to see her again,” Nicky admits.

“Me too,” Rio admits, and the two of them drift into silence as they sit together, both thinking about how much they miss Agatha, how desperate they both are to see her again.

August 2019

Two months have passed since the year Anniversary of Nicky being brough back to life and ever since Nicky has become more determined to learn as much as possible about his magick, reminding Rio more of Agatha with every day that passes.

It’s early on a Thursday morning and just like she did exactly a year ago Rio has stayed up all night to make a birthday cake for her son, one that looks better than the one she made a year before. Just like a year before Rio places candles on top of the cake, though this time it is nine of them, and once the candles are lit, she carries into the room Nicky is sleeping in.

“Nicky, Nicky wake up Mi Conjito,” Rio says as she walks into the room.

“Mommy?” Nicky asks.

“Happy birthday Sweetheart,” Rio says to her son.

“I’m nine!” Nicky says excitedly.

“You are,” Rio confirms, feeling amazed about that fact. “Make a wish,” Rio tells him.

“I know exactly what I’m going to wish for,” Nicky admits, and the truth is Rio does too, so she doesn’t intend to ask what he wished for, before blowing out the candles.

“Nice job,” Rio says, before putting the cake down, cutting a piece for each of them, and once she does that she sits down next to her son, handing him one of the pieces.

“So is birthday cake breakfast in bed becoming a tradition?” Nicky asks curious.

“Yeah, I think so,” Rio confirms, though she knows that Agatha may not approve.

“When’s your birthday, Mom?” Nicky asks curious, as the two of them

“I’ve lived for eternity, I don’t have a birthday,” Rio tells her son, who pouts.

“That’s not fair,” Nicky says. “You should pick a day, and we’ll make that your birthday,” Nicky tells his mother, who knows that while she doesn’t see the point, she doesn’t want to destroy her sons happiness.

“How about you pick one, whatever day you want, we’ll pretend that’s my birthday,” Rio tells Nicky, and for a few moments he looks like he is seriously considering the options before his face breaks out in a grin.

“Halloween,” Nicky tells his mother. “It’s already kind of is, so we should celebrate it as your birthday,” Nicky says.

“Okay,” Rio says with a laugh. “Halloween it is,” Rio confirms.

“Good,” Nicky says before taking a bite of cake.

“So, now that we’ve decided when my birthday is we’ve got to decide what we’re doing today for yours,” Rio tells her son. “We can do anything you want,” Rio tells him.

“Anything?” Nicky asks.

“Within reason,” Rio clarifies, knowing that her version of reason is very different to anyone else, but because Nicky is hers and Agatha’s son adding that stipulation feels necessary. “So, what do you want to do?” Rio asks her son, knowing that she will do whatever she has to do to make what her son wants to do possible.

“Can we try doing the Hexenbesen?” Nicky asks curious. “I really want to fly,” Nicky asks, looking excited about the possibility.

“No,” Rio says, an edge to her voice, surprising Nicky.

“But Mommy, I really want…” Nicky starts to say.

“I said no, Nicholas,” Rio snaps, in a way she has never done with Nicky before.

“I’m sorry,” Nicky says, looking down, and become upset, not understanding what he did wrong.

“Oh Nicky, I’m so sorry,” Rio says, feeling truly awful as she knows that Nicky doesn’t deserve to be snapped at.

“It’s okay, I shouldn’t have asked,” Nicky says, though he is incredibly confused about what he did wrong.

“Nicky, no, you have no reason to apologise, I do, I’m sorry,” Rio says to him. “I never want you to be afraid to ask me anything no matter what it may be,” Rio assures her son, realising that she owes him a story. “Growing up Mama wanted to fly, she wanted the freedom, but her mother,” Rio says, saying the word with more venom than Nicky has ever heard. “Wouldn’t let anyone ever do the Hexenbesen with her,” Rio says, pausing for a moment so she can carefully choose her next words as she knows that Nicky knows practically nothing about his grandmother, and she isn’t quite ready to enlighten him on that particular topic. “After we got together Mama and I would do the Hexenbesen together, we flew a lot, and she would say that it gave her a feeling of freedom she never thought she would have,” Rio says, having long ago added Agatha’s reaction to doing the Hexenbesen to her long list of reasons why she hates Evanora Harkness more than anyone else who has ever existed, and it is also why she used to make excuses for her and Agatha to fly together. “And then when you were a baby Mama would talk about how much she wanted to fly with you when you were old enough,” Rio says, knowing that they didn’t get the chance because Nicky died so young. “Because I can’t find her Mama is missing out on a lot of things with you. She’s missing out on a having a lot of first experiences with you, I’m not going to let your first Hexenbesen be one of them, it means too much to her,” Rio explains to her son, as she cannot do that to Agatha. “So, until we find your mom you’re staying on the ground, okay?” Rio asks.

“Okay,” Nicky says. “I can wait,” Nicky says as while he desperately wants to fly from his moms words, he can tell how important it is to his mama so he will willingly wait until he can do the Hexenbesen with her.

“Thank you,” Rio says. “I know it’s not the same as flying, but how about we go to the beach? We can swim, that’s a little like flying,” Rio says, trying to think of a suitable subsite.

“I’d like that,” Nicky responds.

“Good,” Rio responds, the two of them continue to eat their cake together then proceed to have an amazing day together at the beach.

October 2019

Two months have passed since Nicky’s birthday and even though Rio knows that it is one of the last places in the universe Agatha would go to Rio has brought Nicky to Salem as there are a few things she felt it is important for Nicky to see.

“Welcome to Salem,” Rio says to her son, as the two of them walk around the centre of the town that has been decorated for Halloween, Rio being able to feel that despite Salem’s history there are still a lot of real witches around.

“Okay Mom,” Nicky responds, and he follows behind his mother, feeling curious about where she is going to lead him, but completely trusting her.

About half an hour an hour later, Nicky feeling incredibly curious about where they are going, follows Rio into a clearing, one that she remembered with perfect clarity where it was despite it being difficult to get to location.

“Mom, what is this place?” Nicky asks, as he looks around, sensing something he can’t quiet describe.

“Did you save Mama from her?” Nick asks Rio.

“No, Mama saved herself,” Rio says, smiling fondly as she knows that considering the hell Agatha grew up to it was huge that she managed to break free, even if she couldn’t completely control her magick. “But I considered it a privilege to watch,” Rio admits.

“Mama’s strong,” Nicky says, and Rio isn’t overly sure if that is something he is sensing or just something he is saying.

“The strongest,” Rio says, believing that, and as she says that she notices the way Nicky is looking around. “Nicky?” Rio asks concerned, once again fearing that she has made a mistake by bringing him to this place.

“Can we stay here a little while Mom? I feel Mama here,” Nicky admits, and Rio is sure that that is because of the connection their magick shares, something she can’t completely understand even though she has tried.

“Sure, we could even stay in Salem a little while if you’d like,” Rio tells her son.

“Really?” Nicky asks, looking excited at the possibility.

“Yeah, why not? There were posters in the town about a costume Halloween party next week, we can at least stay for that,” Rio says, as while Salem isn’t her favourite place she can tell that it’s important to Nicky that they spend time in Salem.

“Awesome,” Nicky says with a grin, getting an idea. “Mom, you have to dress up as the Grim Reaper for the party! It would be perfect,” Nicky says to her and Rio laughs.

“We’ll see,” Rio says as she puts an arm around Nicky and kisses the top of his head as the two of them drift into silence as they stand together in the place that has so much significance for them, and their family.

For over a week Rio and Nicky have been staying in Salem, staying in a house that Rio made sure was as far away as possible from the land where Agatha’s childhood home once stood, and it has been clear how much Nicky has enjoyed staying in this particular location.

While Rio would have happily left by now, she has been able to tell that it means a lot to Nicky to be in a place where he can ‘feel’ his mother and because of that they have stayed for longer than Rio has intended, something she now regrets considering what she has just discovered.

Knowing that every second is counts, and that they need to get moving quickly, Rio is hurrying into the room Nicky is sleeping in and quickly tries to wake him up. “Nicky, Nicky, wake up,” Rio says as she shakes her son awake.

“Mom?” Nicky asks, as he wakes up, feeling confused about why his mother would wake him up in the middle of the night.

“We’ve got go move, right now, grab anything you don’t want to leave behind,” Rio says, as she picks up the picture of Agatha that Nicky keeps next to whatever bed he is sleeping in, and puts it into the bag she is holding, having no intention of leaving that behind.

“Mom, what…” Nicky starts to say as he sits up, but then he notices the look on Rio’s face. “You’re scared,” Nicky says shocked, as the only other times he has seen his mother screed was when he was sick and when he died.

After over an hour of carrying her son as she runs Rio finds herself feeling very glad that it takes a lot to tire herself out, but she also feels beyond frustrated with the Salem Seven.

Once Nicky is as safe as he can be, at least temporarily, Rio takes several steps away from her son, not wanting to be close to him when she does what she is about to do, and draws on her concentration, her power.  Muttering a language that not another being speaks Rio lifts her arms, brings them to her chest, then pushes them out, and as she does an incredible force of magick is released from her, a force that even Nicky can tell is strong.

In the seconds that follow Rio letting out an incredibly strong force the magick echoes throughout the forest and causes every living thing, except for Nicky who is protected, and Rio herself, to be made dormmate either, in the case of human or animal being made unconscious, or in the case of any other living thing being made dormmate.

After releasing her power Rio has to spend a few seconds collecting herself, as there is a reason she only does that as a last resort, before walking over to her son, who can practically ‘feel’ the power radiating off her, something he has never felt before.

As soon as Nicky sticks out his arm Rio sees that he has a decent cut on it, something which likely happened as he fell to the ground. “Oh, that’s nothing, I can fix that right up,” Rio says, as she lifts Nicky’s arm to her mouth and places gentle kisses along the wound on her son’s arm, using her own healing ability to heal it. “Better?” Rio asks.

“Good, them let’s get out of here,” Rio says before picking up her son and the bag that were dropped.

Across the world the person Nicky and Rio want to see most, Agatha Harkness, is sitting alone in a basement studying the Darkhold, as she obsessively reads, flicking the pages with her blackened fingers, she feels a force so strong that she has to stop what she is doing as she tries to catch her breath.

“Rio,” Agatha mutters, being able to identify exactly who is the source of the magick, as she knows it just as well as she knows her own, and for a brief second she finds herself wondering just what her estranged wife is up to. “Not my problem,” Agatha says, as she doesn’t want to see Rio, doesn’t want to deal with her, even if a part of her can’t help but wonder if she is okay, but she pushes those feelings down and instead goes back to reading the book that calls to her having no idea that if she were to investigate what she just felt she would find exactly what she is searching the Darkhold for.

Days have passed since Rio woke up Nicky in the middle of the night due to the Salem Seven and ever since she and Nicky have been running. While Rio has been doing her best to limit how many times, they stop it has been necessary to stop more than she would like due to the effects the magick she performed has on her.

Gaining access to a house in Alaska Rio knows that they need to take time to rest, even if she would prefer to keep going and as neither she nor Nicky have sensed anything that tells them that the Salem Seven are still following them since they left Massachusetts, she knows it’s time.

“Are we going to stay here?” Nicky asks his mother.

“For a little while,” Rio says, knowing that she desperately needs a few hours to rest before they can move on again.

“Are we safe here, Mom?” Nicky asks, and Rio tenses, knowing they have to have a difficult conversation, one she was hoping they wouldn’t have to have to have until Nicky was a little older, but now that the Salem Seven are in play she knows it’s time.

“Let’s sit down, Nicky,” Rio says to her son, and she leads him over the couch, where they both sit down. “Nicky, you know I am always going to do whatever I have to do to keep you safe, and that when we find Mama she will to?” Rio asks her son.

“I know,” Nicky responds.

“I wish, and I know Mama would too, that I could promise you that you’d always be safe, but the truth is I can’t,” Rio tells her son. “Because of who you are, because of who we all are and what we can do, we’re always going to be in danger, always going to have people who hate us, who want to hurt us,” Rio tells her son, knowing that there is a few different layers to that, but it’s not the time to address that. “Me, and Mama when we find her, are always going to do whatever we have to do to keep you safe. We’ll give everything we are to making sure you are okay, but even with how powerful we are there are things we can’t prevent, things we can’t keep from happening or protect you from,” Rio tells her son.

“Like when I died,” Nicky says, and Rio has to fight back tears at that reminder.

“Exactly like that,” Rio says, fighting to keep her voice even. “But that doesn’t mean we’re going to give up, it doesn’t mean we’re going to stop trying to protect you, it just means that sometimes we have to fight a little harder,” Rio admits, before leaning forward. “But you know what, I have been fighting for Mama for over three hundred years, I’m not going to stop now, and neither of us will ever stop fighting for you,” Rio assures her son.

“I’m going to fight for you and Mama too,” Nicky promises his mother.

“I know you will,” Rio says, smiling slightly. “That’s exactly what we have to keep doing, Nicky, keep fighting for each other, keep fighting for our family, to be safe, and if we do that maybe, just maybe we can keep ahead of the people who want to hurt us and have longer moments where we are safe,” Rio says to her son.

“I think we can do it,” Nicky says. “You, me, Mama, we’re strong,” Nicky says to Rio, who once again wonders if Nicky can ‘sense’ magick as that’s what it is beginning to seem like to her.

“Sure,” Nicky says and together mother and son perform ancient, powerful, magick designed to keep them safe while Rio regains her strength.

December 2019

Two months have passed since Rio and Nicky ran from the Salem Seven and to Rio’s relief there hasn’t been anything that indicates they might still be following them. As she knows they cannot afford to get complacence Rio is still moving them frequently, trying to put as much distance between them and Salem as possible.

What are you thinking?” Rio asks.

May 2020

About three months have passed since Rio told Nicky to do whatever he wants to do while she keeps them safe and ever since he has taken that to heart, spending most of his time studying every magickal book Rio is about to get him while also learning languages and cooking. In fact, he has become so interested in his studies that most nights he falls asleep with a book in his hands. Even though it is late at night Nicky isn’t asleep, in fact he isn’t even reading, rather he is walking around the house he and Nicky have been staying at in Brazil.

Having no idea that Nicky is so worried about her, though she suspects he might be considering how long she has returned, Rio is finally arriving back at the house in Brazil Nicky has been staying in and as she walks into the house the first thing, she realises is that she smells a lot of food.
