August 2020

About three months have passed since Rio had to be gone for longer than she expected and for the first little while Rio noticed that Nicky clung to her more when she was home but after a few weeks of her returning quickly when she left, he has been doing a lot better.

It’s Nicky’s tenth birthday and after starting their day with their traditional cake in bed Nicky and Rio have gone outside to the backyard of the Cottage, which is where they are staying, because Nicky wants to show his mother what he has been learning.

“Mom, are you watching?” Nicky asks his mother, as he stands several steps away from Rio.

“Of course, Mi Conejito,” Rio assures her son.

“Great,” Nicky says, sounding glad.

For the next few minutes Nicky demonstrates blasting, levitating as well as several spells that he has been practicing before walking back over to where his mother is.

“What do you think?” Nicky asks his mother.

“I think you’ve got some pretty impressive Magick Mi Conejito,” Rio assures her son, and Nicky grins. “And I never want you to be ashamed of your power, or talent, but you need to be careful, magick can be dangerous,” Rio tells him, trying to find the delicate balance between wanting to make sure Nicky is never ashamed of his powers and wanting to make sure he is safe. “Magick can make people think you are dangerous,” Rio reminds him, thinking of Agatha and knowing that Agatha would never want what happened to her to happen to their son.

“I know, I’ll be careful,” Nicky assures his mother.

“Good,” Rio says, and as she does, she gets an idea. “So, it looks like you’re starting to get a handle om your magick,” Rio says, sounding proud, before pulling her knife. “How would you feel about learning some other ways to protect yourself? Other ways to fight?” Rio asks curious, as she wants to make sure her son is a prepared as possible for what might come after him, which she knows could be a lot the biggest thing on her mind being that just because the Salem 7 haven’t caught up with them again doesn’t mean they won’t.

“I’d love that,” Nicky admits.

“Great,” Rio says before easily moving through the gaps in the fence so that she can stand next to her son. “We’re starting with some basic moves, then we’ll move onto knifes,” Rio tells Nicky, purposely not thinking about what Agatha would say if she knew Rio was teaching their ten-year-old son how to use knives.

“Awesome,” Nicky says, with a huge grin on his face, and after returning her son’s grin Rio proceeds to get started on her lesson.

November 2020

Three months have passed since Rio started to teach Nicky other ways to defend himself and just like when learning everything else, he has dedicated everything he is to learning, to being as good as he can.

Having spent the last few hours taking the souls of people who died in a pretty bad skirmish, which involved a lot of kids getting caught in the crossfire, Rio is very glad to be returning home to Nicky, as that’s what she knows, that no matter how many times they have to move wherever Nicky, and Agatha, are that’s where she considers to be her home.

Walking into the most current house they are staying in Rio finds that once again there is a lot of food on the table, something which is surprising as she hasn’t been gone overly long.

“Nicky, what’s all this?” Rio asks her son.

“I know there are certain foods you like to eat more than others, so I thought I would make them all for you,” Nicky explains to his mother. “I wanted to do something special for you,” Nicky says and because she has a suspicion about why Nicky would feel the need to make something special for her Rio knows she needs to make sure.

“Nicky, why do you think I need something special?” Rio asks curious.

“Because I know you had to take a lot of people to where they needed to be today,” Nicky tells his mother, confirming what Rio suspected but that doesn’t make it any easier to hear.

“I did,” Rio confirms, before walking over to her son and hugging him. “You’re pretty incredible, Mi Conejito, I love you so much,” Rio says hugging her son tightly.

“Love you too, Mom,” Nicky responds, and the two of them continue to stand in the room hugging as while, Rio taking comfort from her son as while she doesn’t usually find doing her job difficult when it involves children it is different; something which Nicky has obviously realises.

March 2021

About four months has passed since Nicky realised his mom had a difficult time doing her job and since then it has become clear that he can, for lack of a better term, ‘sense death’ in different ways, but to Rio’s relief when it comes to knowing if a specific person is going to die, he has to touch them first.

“You know you never told me why you wanted to come here today,” Rio tells her son as the two of them are walking through a street in Hong Kong, too close for Rio’s liking to the Hong Kong Sanctum; a place whose inhabitants she doesn’t want to be anywhere near her son.

“It feels like somewhere I need to be today,” Nicky admits, sounding uncertain about exactly why and because of that Rio freezes as she knows that he would be feeling that for one of two reasons. While she is surprised by her son’s words Rio only allows herself a few seconds to feel that shock before she gets her baring’s and squats down in front of her son.

“Nicky, I need you to talk to me, are you sensing that a lot of people are going to die her or that a lot of magick is going to be used here?” Rio asks her son, wanting to know exactly what they are going to be facing.

“Both,” Nicky answers. “I want to help,” Nicky admits, and Rio has to pause to control her reaction to that.

“No,” Rio tells her son. “We’ve got to go,” Rio says knowing that she needs to get Nicky to safety before he decides to intervene

“But Mom…..” Nicky starts to say.

“But nothing, we’re going,” Rio says, standing up and grabbing her son’s hand. “Now, Nicholas,” Rio tells her son, but before they can even take a few steps there is a large magickal explosion at the Sanctum, and Rio knows immediately that people have died. “Don’t even think about it,” Rio says, looking at her son and seeing the look on his face which tells her that he is about to run straight into a situation without thinking, knowing the look perfectly because she has seen an identical one on Agatha’s face countless times.

“I want to help,” Nicky tells his mother. “I want them to know that it will be okay, that you’ll take them where they need to go,” Nicky tells his mother. “That it’s okay,” Nicky tells his mother.

“People aren’t ready to hear that this soon after a tragedy,” Rio tells her son, experience telling her that much. “We’re going,” Rio tells her son.

“But your job…” Nicky starts to say.

“Will still need to be done once I get you to safety,” Rio says, and before he can object further, she picks up her son, something she wouldn’t be able to do if she was just a regular human, and carries him away from the magickal battle that is going on.

A little while after she carried Nicky away from the battle the two of them, Nicky still being in Rio’s arms as she has no intention of letting him go until she is sure that he can’t follow, are arriving back at the house they are staying at.

“I could just follow you Mom,” Nicky says annoyed, as his mother puts him on the ground.

“No, you can’t,” Rio tells her son, and feeling glad that she had the foresight not to teach her son a particular protection, a particular rune, that will keep him in the house and make it so he can’t follow her, she casts it knowing that Nicky won’t be able to break it. “We’ll be talking about this when I get back,” Rio tells her son before teleporting away, and the second she goes Nicky tries to leave the house so he can follow but he quickly realises he can’t.

“Mom! Mom! Damn it! I just want to reassure people,” Nicky says annoyed, before going to where he can keep his books so he can start to figure out what his mother has done to keep him where he is.

While her mind is solely on Nicky, Rio is attempting to do her job, but with every soul she fairs to the other side her mind just keeps going back to Nicky, and Agatha, to the undeniable truth that she can’t keep raising their son alone, that she needs Agatha, that Rio alone isn’t enough for Nicky.

After Rio fairies the last soul who died to the veil, she returns to the battle, not searching for more people who she needs to fairy but trying to figure out what to do next because she honestly doesn’t know how she is going to help her son, isn’t sure what she can do for him.

Looking around even Rio can feel the power that has been used in location, though unlike Nicky, she can only feel it now that it has happened, something which makes her realise something.

“He got that from Agatha,” Rio says, coming to her realisation and as she does, she starts to get an idea. “Worth a try,” Rio says, as she has no idea what else to do, she is completely out of ideas.

Walking over to a wall, where there is a strong ‘sense’ of magick, Rio leaves a trace of her magick, as well as message that only Agatha would be able to find, saying; ‘ find me, we need to talk. It’s important’ .

For a moment Rio debates saying something about Nicky, but because she doesn’t want to risk someone else finding about it, she doesn’t, she just hopes that this magical battle was interesting enough for Agatha to come look into, and more than that she hopes that if she does Agatha doesn’t ignore the message; something which she knows is a long shot.

“Please Agatha, please, stop hiding,” Rio says, as a tear comes to her eyes, having a desperate need to see her again. “I can’t keep doing this without you,” Rio admits, and after spending a few moments collecting herself, as she doesn’t want Nicky to realise that she is sad, Rio makes her way back to where she left her son.

Arriving at the house Rio lifts the protection she put in place to keep Nicky where he was and makes her way inside, considering the way they left things Rio isn’t at all surprised to find that Nicky isn’t there to great her in the way he usually would.

With a sigh Rio takes a few calming breaths, getting a feeling that she is going to need it for this particular conversion, and heads into the room that Nicky has been staying and considering the way she knows her son can be like Rio isn’t at all surprised to find him sitting on the ground, surrounded by books.

“You still mad at me?” Rio asks from the doorway, suspecting that if he can hold a grudge like his Mama then he will be.

“Yes… no…. I don’t know,” Nick admits, and feeling that that is as good of an answer that she is going to get Rio walks over to him and finds a place among the books to sit down. “I just wanted to help,” Nicky tells his mother. “I knew there was a lot of magick, and that people were going to die, that nothing could change that, but I thought I still thought I could help, give them some peace,” Nicky admits.

“That’s not your responsibility, Mi Conejito,” Rio tells her son. “I am so proud of you for wanting to help, but Nicky you cannot keep things this serious from me, you cannot manipulate what we do like you just did,” Rio tells her son. “Nicky, we were near an organization who would try to make you conform to their version of magick if they knew about you, there was incredible amounts of power released, and it was being used in dangerous ways, if you tried to use your magcks people could realise who you are, you have no idea how dangerous what you just did is,” Rio tells her son, trying to keep her voice even, but feeling completely terrified that her son was going to do something so dangerous without thinking about it.

“Isn’t the danger worth it if I could help people?” Nicky asks.

“Not to me,” Rio tells her son. “Nicky, I can’t lose you again,” Rio says, her voice breaking, knowing that even with how powerful she is that is something she couldn’t survive a second time. “Please, if you feel something like this again talk to me first, and we’ll figure out what to do, together,” Rio say, and Nicky can tell how upset his mother is becoming at that.

“Okay Mom,” Nicky says, before leaning forward and hugging his mother, realising that he scared her. “I’ll talk to you next time,” Nicky says.

“Thank you,” Rio says as she hugs her son, kissing the top of his head, as she holds her son close, desperately hoping that Agatha gets her message, while Nicky has no idea what he can do to help his mom who is clearly not okay.

August 2021

About five months have passed since Nicky was able to sense a deadly magic battle before it happened and since then he hasn’t experienced anything just like that but what he has realised is what something else he is sensing is. As well as realising that he is sensing Nicky, who has recently turned eleven, has also realised that his mother is struggling that she is not okay, and he knows that the only thing that would be able to help her is finding Agatha.

Having just finished escorting an elderly couple, who died within moments of each other, to the veil Rio is just returning to the latest house they are living in. Walking into the house Rio finds Nicky sitting in the middle of the living room in a meditation pose.

“Nicky?” Rio asks hesitantly, not seeing any magic around him so she isn’t certain exactly what her son is doing.

“Hi Mom,” Nicky says, opening his eyes, and when he does Rio sees a flicker of blue.

“What were you just doing?” Rio asks curious, and as she asks her question, she can tell that Nicky is nervous to answer. “Nicky, you can talk to me, always, no matter what,” Rio assures her son, as she walks over and sits down on the floor in front of him.

“I know,” Nicky says as he is sure that no matter what he can always talk to his mom. “I just… I just don’t want to make you sadder than you already are,” Nicky admits, and Rio is surprised by that as while she has been sad lately, she thought she was doing a good job at keeping it form Nicky.

“Why do you think I’m, sad Mi Conejito?” Rio asks her son.

“I heard you crying,” Nicky admits. “I know you miss Mama; I know it hurts you to know we can’t find her, that we can’t be together,” Nicky tells his mother.

“It does,” Rio admits. “Nicky I am doing everything I can to find Mama, but sometimes knowing we can’t find her, knowing everything you two are missing out on because I can’t, it hurts,” Rio admits.

“That’s why I’m trying to help,” Nicky admits.

“Nicky, what are you trying to do?” Rio asks curious.

“I’ve always felt something, it feels familiar, safe, and it’s something that I have always just felt, like it’s apart of me,” Nicky explains, having no idea if the explanation is making sense, but it is the best explanation he can give. “After Hong Kong I realised what it is I’m feeling, it’s Mama,” Nicky reveals, smiling fondly. “It’s the connection our magic shares, she’s always been with me, and I didn’t even realise,” Nicky says, feeling comforted by that thought, not knowing that the only reason Agatha isn’t feeling the same thing is the Darkhold’s influence.

“Nicky, do you know where she is?” Rio asks, feeling hope that maybe they are closer to finding Agatha than she released.

“No, I’m sorry Mom,” Nicky admits. “That’s what I have been trying to do, getting enough focus so that I can find Mama, but I can’t tell where she is, all I can tell is that she is out there,” Nicky admits, not realising that like his mom his ability to find his mama is being hampered by the Darkhold, and its influence. “I’m so sorry Mom,” Nicky admits, feeling that he is letting his mother down.

“Oh Mi Conejito, you have nothing to apologize for, okay, absolutely nothing,” Rio assures her son before hugging him tight, feeling amazed at what he is trying to do. “We’ll figure it out, we’ll find her, I know we will,” Rio says, that being something she needs to believe right now, and for a moment mother and son just hold each other, both feeling the missing piece that should be with them.

February 2022

Six months have passed since Nicky first tried to use his magic to figure out where his mother is, something he has continued to regularly try but due to the Darkhold, something he doesn't know, he hasn't been able to. What Nicky does know is that he keeps failing and from his perspective it feels like he is just letting his moms down, something which Rio frequently assures him isn't the case but witch he cannot believe.

After his latest attempt at trying to determine where his Mama is failed Nicky felt the need to escape the small house in Poland he and his mom have been staying in, he felt the need to be around actual people, and because of that he did something he has never done before, he lowered the protections his mother puts around the house when she's not home, and left.

Heading into the nearby village Nicky spends a few hours just being around regular people, he plays games at a little fair that is going on, and he even goes on a couple of rides. Despite what it may seem like after what he did Nicky has enough sense to know that he can't stay away from where his mother will expect to find him for long.

Returning to the house Nicky suspects that he may have just gotten away with leaving the protection without his mother realizing when just as he is about to open the front door his mother appears not too far away.

"Hi Mom," Nicky greats, trying to figure out if his mother realized he lowered the protections.

"You sound just like your Mama when you use that tone of voice," Rio informs Nicky, immediately feeling suspicious about what he was up to.

"Thank you," Nicky says with a grin, considering it a compliment. "I was thinking we could make hamburgers for dinner, what do you think?" Nicky asks his mother curious, clearly trying to change the subject to distract her from realizing what he did to the protections.

"I think we're going to have a chat about why you lowered the protections," Rio tells her son. "Sit," Rio says, gesturing to the stairs, and Nicky sits down. "What's going on?" Rio asks his son, not moving straight to reminding her son why that was such a bad idea because she wants to hear his reasons.

"I just… felt a little stir crazy and that I needed to be around other people," Nicky admits. "I know it was dangerous to lower the protections, to leave, but I just… needed not to be alone for a little while, I needed to do something around other people," Nicky admits, having no idea how his mother is going to respond to that.

"Nicky, I'm sorry," Rio tells her son.

"Why are you apologizing?" Nicky asks confused.

"Because I'm keeping you away from the entire world," Rio tells her son. "I do need to keep you safe; I will do anything I can to do that, but I've forgotten that living means actually doing things that make you feel alive," Rio admits, feeling worried that she has been focusing so much on protecting Nicky that she forgets that. "Nicky sometimes because of who I am I don't think about the fact that humans need contact with other humans, that you will need to spend time with people, and I'm sorry about that," Rio tells her son.

"It's okay Mom, I'd say you're doing a pretty good job at considering things for me that you don't have to consider for yourself," Nicky assures his mother, who knows that this is just another example of why they need Agatha, who so far has continued to ignore the messages Rio has left her.

"Thank you," Rio says, not overly sure she can forgive herself even if Nicky understands. "So, how about instead of having dinner here tonight we go find a place in town to have it," Rio suggests.

"I'd like that," Nicky responds. "If you're interested there is a fair in town, with an annoying game, I was trying and failing to win something at," Nicky tells his mother, knowing he was very close to trying magic. "Do you want to give it a try?" Nicky asks his mother.

"Sure," Rio says with a smirk. "I don't know if I've told you, but Death always wins the game," Rio tells her son as they both stand up, Nicky laughing as he does.

"That was pretty lame, Mom," Nicky informs her.

"I thought it was pretty great," Rio responds, as the two of them head towards the village together, where they proceed to spend time at the fair, where Nicky is sure his mother cheated at games, before having dinner.

August 2022

Almost six months have passed since Rio realized Nicky needs to actually spend time with regular people and ever since she has been doing her best to find a balance between what is necessary to protect him and what is necessary for his wellbeing.

It is Nicky's twelve birthday and Rio is once again thinking about how it's something else Agatha is missing, something which Rio only blames herself for because she hates that she is meant to be all powerful and yet she can't find Agatha because of a damn book.

"Mom, are you going to tell me where we are going anytime soon?" Nicky asks his mother as after their usual birthday tradition of eating birthday cake in bed Rio rushed them into the car and the two of them have been driving for a while.

"You'll see soon," Rio tells her son, as she continues to drive them through a California highway in the white convertible she obtained for this special occasion.

"Okay," Nicky responds, looking around.

"Trust me, Mi Conejito, you're gonna have a great time," Rio assures her son.

"I do trust you, Mom, always," Nicky says, smiling at his mother.

For another fifteen or so minutes Rio continues to drive and while Nicky is confused about where they are going his confusion lifts when he sees exactly where they are going.

"We're going to Six Flags, Magic Mountain?" Nicky asks amazed.

"Yep," Rio confirms. "I thought we could have some fun, see if there are any rollercoasters that are actually scary," Rio admits, knowing that both of them very much enjoy doing things that some point would consider them being 'thrill seekers'.

"Sounds like a plan," Nicky says with a grin. "Can I ride anything?" Nicky asks.

"As long as you meet the height requirements," Rio tells Nicky, not expecting that to be a problem, but wanting to make that exception clear as she won't let him do something that isn't safe for him.

"Awesome," Nicky says with a grin, and the two of them proceed to celebrate Nicky's birthday by riding as many scary rides as possible.

December 2022

Four months have passed since Nicky's twelve birthday and while Rio is trying to keep it together, it is clear that they are both struggling more with the fact that they haven't been able to find Agatha. While Rio is blaming herself because she feels like she is letting down both Agatha and Nicky, Nicky is blaming himself because he can feel the connection his magic shares with Agatha and yet he still can't feel where she is; something he doesn't realize isn't his fault.

It's late and Rio is returning to Nicky after doing her job. Just like she does every time she returns Rio goes straight to the room where Nicky is sleeping to make sure he is okay. As quietly opens the door to the room Nicky is in Rio finds that he is not sleeping like he usually would be, but rather he is lying in bed, crying.

"Nicky?" Rio asks, worried, as she quicky turns on the light and walks over to him. "Nicky, talk to me," Rio says in a gentle voice as she sits down on the edge of the bed.

"We're not going to find Mama are we?" Nicky asks, voicing what he has been fearing for a while, as he looks at Rio.

"I… honestly… I don't know," Rio admits, it breaking her heart to say that. "I know we're not going to give up, and I know what I believe," Rio admits.

"What's that?" Nicky asks curious.

"That Mama and I have been pulling off impossible things, both together and apart, for over three hundred years, and because of that I believe we're going to find her," Rio admits. "I just don't know if we're going to find her soon, but that being said I truly believe we will find her," Rio tells Nicky, not sure if she is causing Nicky harm by being so optimistic about finding Agatha, but she doesn't want him to give up hope because she knows she never will.

"I want to believe….. I just really want Mama," Nicky admits, his voice breaking, tears rolling down his face.

"Me too," Rio says, pulling Nicky up and into her arms, and holding him tight as Nicky breaks down in in her arms, Rio feeling angry that Agatha is still hidden from them, heartbreak that Nicky is so upset, and also her own heartbreak about the fact that they haven't been able to find Agatha even though they have been searching for almost five years.

May 2023

Five months have passed since Nicky broke down in his mother's arms because he is losing hope about finding Agatha again and while he is trying to have the same optimism as his mom, he is finding it a little harder to believe that they will find her.

Having spent a few hours doing her job during the day rather than at night, something which Rio doesn't like to do often, she is returning home to the house she and Nicky are staying at in Wales.

"Nicky?" Rio asks, as she returns home and sees no sing of him, and she can feel that the protections were lowered. "NICHOLAS VIDAL-HARKNESS?" Rio yells through the house, panic rising up inside of her, and as she does, she notices a piece of paper on the table. Hurrying over to the note Rio quickly picks it up so she can read it.

Mom,

Don't worry, I'm fine. There's a library two miles south that has an amazing collection of occult books. I don't know if they are actually real books, but I needed to check. I'm okay, I have the knife you gave me, and I will pay attention to everything around me. Hope your job wasn't too hard. Love you,

Nicky

"Damn it, Nicky," Rio mutters, as while she appreciates Nicky's desire to know more, and she knows he want to learn as much as possible she can't help but worry as she knows how much danger her son is in.

Needing to know that her son is okay Rio drops the note Nicky left and goes running out of the house, wanting to get to the library as quickly as possible, as while she knows she has done everything she can to make sure Nicky can protect himself she can't help but worry about him.

Not long after she arrived home to find Nicky gone Rio is arriving at the library and while her magick doesn't connect to Nicky in the same way Nicky and Agatha's magicks are connected as soon as she walks into the library Rio knows where he is.

Following the feeling Rio finds Nicky sitting in a corner of the library surrounded by books, clearly concentrating hard, and as she sees him Rio has to pause for a second because she can't help but reminded of just how much he looks like Agatha when he is like that.

Feeling relieved that Nicky is seemingly okay Rio spends a few moments watching her son before walking over to him, sitting down next to him, putting her legs up on the table as she does.

"Hi Mom," Nicky greats.

"Don't hi mom me, what were you thinking?" Rio asks.

"I left a note," Nicky says in his defense.

"Not good enough," Rio tells him. "Nicky, if you want to go somewhere while I'm gone you need to tell me first, okay, unless I have a very good reason I won't say no. I need to know where you are so I don't arrive home and panic because I can't find you and then I think that the Salem Seven or one of our other enemies have gotten to you," Rio explains, as that's where her mind went to when she couldn't find Nicky, that something awful had happened.

"I didn't think of it like that," Nicky admits, feeling bad, as he realizes he should have. "Sorry Mom, I'll tell you next time," Nicky says to her.

"Thank you," Rio says relieved. "So, found anything interesting?" Rio asks curious.

"Maybe," Nicky says, searching the books he was reading to pick up a specific one which he shows Rio. "Was this Mama?" Nicky asks, as he hands the book to Rio, who quickly reads something that happened in 1780.

"Yeah, it was," Rio says with a laugh, remembering what happened and after checking to make sure no one is nearby to overhear Rio proceeds to tell her son the story, at least the PG version of the story.

October 2023

Five months have passed since Nicky and Rio agreed that Nicky could go places when she is doing her job but only if they talked about it first and in in that Nicky has turned thirteen and Rio has made even more of an effort to leave messages for Agatha trying to get her to contact her, something which Agatha hasn't done yet.

As she has just felt the feeling of five Infinity Stones being used at the same time for the second time in her existence Rio is once again feeling the universe in chaos, but that is nothing compared to the fear she is feeling.

Stopping what she is doing mid-job Rio makes her way back to the Cottage as quickly as possible as she has only one thing on her mind as she feels everyone who were snapped away five years ago come back.

"NICKY!" Rio yells as she hurries into the house, being able to hear her heart beating in her ears, feeling terrified that because those who were lost five years ago were brought back her son who she was able to get back because of the chaos will be taken away again.

"Mom?" Nicky asks, running out of the bedroom. "Are you okay?" Nicky asks, but he has barely gotten the question out before his mother is pulling him into his her arms, holding him tightly.

"Mom, I'm okay," Nicky assures her. "I haven't gone anywhere," Nicky assures her. "You're worried because of that power surge, aren't you?" Nicky asks, as that's what he assumes.

"You felt that?" Rio asks worried, as she breaks apart from her son to look at him, not overly surprised because she knows that Nicky can sense magic, but considering how strong it was for her she is worried about the effect it would have on her son.

"Yeah, it was… lot… overwhelming…. It felt like I couldn't breathe for a few second," Nicky admits.

"I'm really sorry you felt that," Rio admits and as she does, because of what she is feeling bubbling below her surface she knows what she has to do, but she cannot do it alone. "Nicky, I need your help," Rio tells her son.

"Of course, Mom," Nicky says to her. "What do you need?" Nicky asks his mother.

"There's about to be a lot of death, a huge battle that will include a lot of magic. So, I need your help to cast a spell that will temporarily make this cottage out of phase with reality, that way I can do my job without being overwhelming and that will allow me to focus without being affected by the chaos that is currently going on, and that may happen again if whoever has the infinity stones use them again," Rio explain. "It will protect you from both what you can sense and anything else that happens," Rio explains.

"I can help," Nicky assures his mother, being able to tell how serious this is.

"Thank you," Rio tells her son, feeling grateful. "Here's what we have to do," Rio says before starting to explain to her son exactly what they are going to do, something which they are the only ones who can do as they are the only two beings, in the universe, who speak the language they need to use.

November 2023

Just over three weeks have passed since everyone who snapped away was brought back and both Rio and Nicky are dealing with the effects of that. Rio is dealing with more work as the entire world is in chaos once again, while Nicky is still feeling a little overwhelmed due to the effects that sensing infinity stones being used more than once had on him; despite Rio's attempt to prevent that with the spell they cast.

It's early morning at the cottage, where Rio and Nicky have been staying since the blip, as it's being called, and the two of them are having breakfast together.

"Do you have more of an appetite today?" Rio asks her son, still trying to understand just what effects sensing the infinity stones being used multiple times is having on her son.

"A little, but not much," Nicky admits. "I do feel like I'm getting more energy back," Nicky admits.

"Good that's good," Rio says, and once she does both, she and Nicky feel the exact same thing at the same time.

"Agatha," Rio says, with an amazed look on her face, bringing her hand up to her heart, at the exact same time Nicky says, "Mama,".

Chapter 8

AN : Thank you for the absolutely amazing response to the last chapter. I hope I live up to your expectations, I’m a little nervous. Please let me know what you think.

“You can feel Mama too?” Nicky asks his mother, as while he has gotten used to being able to feel his mother that feeling just got a whole lot stronger.

“Yeah,” Rio says, feeling amazed as it is has been so long since she has been able to feel Agatha, and it has truly felt like she lost a part of herself when she stopped being able to feel her, but now she feels like she has gotten that piece back. “I know where she is,” Rio says, knowing this is everything she has wanted, but as she feels that she also feels something else. “Something’s not right,” Rio realises, her face falling, feeling dread rise up inside of her.

“Mom, is she….” Nicky starts to ask as even he can ‘feel’ that there is something off with what he is feeling, but he doesn’t know what it means, and he is scared to ask.

“She’s alive,” Rio says, knowing that without a doubt. “But something’s not right,” Rio admits, not sure exactly what she is feeling but knowing that whatever it is ‘less’ Agatha in a sense.

“Then let’s go,” Nicky says, standing up. “Let’s get to Mama,”

“Not until you eat,” Rio says as while everything she is wants to go after Agatha immediately, she knows that she needs to make sure Nicky is looked after.

“But Mom…” Nicky starts to object.

“But nothing, we’re going to have to travel across the world to get to Mama, we can’t do that if you pass out because you haven’t eaten,” Rio tells her son. “Eat, then we can collect what we need and go,” Rio says, giving her son a look which Nicky has learnt to mean ‘you’re not going to fight me on this,’.

“Fine,” Nicky says annoyed, and he reluctantly sits down and tries to eat, feeling amazed that he is finally going to get to see his mama again.

After three days of traveling, it having taken longer than either would like because Rio can’t teleport with Nicky, and she refuses to use brooms without Agatha, Rio and Nicky are finally using a car Rio has ‘obtained’ to drive into Westview New Jersey; the location they both know they will find Agatha.

“Mom, what do you think happened here?” Nicky asks, as the drive through the town centre and they see a lot of military vehicles, vehicles marked with an acronym SWORD, and as well as what he can see Nicky also feels that a lot of magic has been used.

“I’m not sure, but it has to be why Mama was here,” Rio admits, knowing that would make sense. “I know she’s here, in town, but I can’t tell exactly where she is,” Rio admits, feeling extremely concerned that she can’t tell exactly where Agatha is. “Can you?” Rio asks her son, still trying to make sense of the connection Agatha and Nicky’s magicks share.

“No,” Nicky says, shaking his head. “It’s like there’s too much interference, I have never felt anything like it,” Nicky admits, wondering just what it is that he is feeling.

“Okay, we do this the old fashion way then,” Rio says, parking the car away from where the government cars are. “Come on,” Rio tells her son, and they both get out of the car.

Feeling curious about what his mother is going to do Nicky gets out of the car and follows Rio as she approaches two ladies who are together talking.

“I’m sorry, I am hoping you can help me,” Rio says to the ladies, putting on a very ‘panicked’ voice to try and get help as she figures it will be her best option. “I’m looking for someone very important to me, I was told she is here,” Rio explains. “He name’s Agatha, Agatha Harkness,” Rio explains.

“I’m sorry, I don’t know anyone by that name,” The woman, Sharon Davis, says, and Rio feels her heart sink. “But that doesn’t mean she isn’t here,” Sharon explains, noticing Rio’s reaction, and wanting to make her feel better.

“Okay, um, she’s around my height, beautiful, has long dark hair, blue eyes that look like a storm,” Rio starts to explain, and Nicky can’t help but give his mother a surprised look at hearing her describe his mama like that. “Really loves the colour purple,” Rio says, knowing that there are a thousand other ways she could describe Agatha, but that seems like the best way.

“Oh, that sounds like Agnes!” Sharon explains, and both Rio and Nicky feel hope at that. “She helped us all,” Sharon explains.

“Really?” Nicky asks, feeling proud.

“Where can I find Agnes?” Rio asks, before anyone can address what Nicky asked, being sure there is a bigger story.

“She’s lives over on Sherwood drive, number 2804,” Sharon explains. “Um, she is having some problems knowing who she is right now,” Sharon admits, feeling the need to give that warning.

“I’m sure I will be able to remind her,” Rio says, believing that, believing that, before walking away without another word.

“Thank you,” Nicky says to Sharon before running to catch up with his mother. “Do you think whatever is causing Mama problems knowing who she is why we can’t sense her?” Nicky asks his mother in a quiet voice.

“I don’t know,” Rio admits. “Something big has happened here,” Rio admits, looking around, as the two of them get back in the car.

“Definitely seems like it,” Nicky confirms, as the two of them get back into the car.

As it’s such a full town Rio has no problem finding Sherwood drive, and no problem finding the house, which Rio stops the car outside of, but to Nicky’s confusion even though Rio stops the car she doesn’t make an effort to get out.

“Mom?” Nicky asks concerned.

“She’s not going to want to see me,” Rio admits, and Nicky can tell that his mother is hurt by that.

“You don’t know that,” Nicky tells his mother, trying to be encouraging.

“I do,” Rio admits, her voice breaking, as she has been so focused on getting Nicky to Agatha, she hasn’t let herself think about what it means for her and Agatha, how Agatha is going to respond to seeing her again.

“Well, what I know is that Mama is right here, we’re finally so close to being back together, you can’t let your fear hold you back now, Mom,” Nicky says, as he takes off his seatbelt an opening the door. “You coming or not?” Nicky says as he gets out of the car.

“Nicky, wait,” Rio says as she quickly gets out of the car and hurries over to where he is walking up the path. “Just let me do the talking first, okay?” Rio says, as the two of them continue to walk up the path.

“Okay,” Nicky nods.

“And if we start fighting, just stay out our way, it’s often how we say hello,” Rio admits, not wanting Nicky to think something is wrong, or to get in the crosshairs, if she and Agatha start fighting, something which is very strong possibility.

“I’m not even going to try to unpack that,” Nicky admits, though he has a lot of questions

“Good choice,” Rio tells her son, as they reach the front door.

“Do you want me to knock?” Nicky asks, as his mother makes no effort to move towards the door.

“No, I will,” Rio says, and she hesitantly reaches out and knocks on the door, not breaking it down like she is tempted to because she doesn’t know what to expect, and as it feels like every second lasts an eternity they wait until the door opens.

As soon as Agatha opens the door, and Rio sees her for the first time in 153 years, Rio knows two things without a doubt, the first is that Agatha is just as beautiful as last time she saw her, and the second is the way she is dressed is very unlike Agatha.

“Howdy Neighbours, can I help you?” Agatha, who unknown to Rio and Nicky is trapped under a persona of Anges O’Connor, asks in an overly friendly tone of voice, as she looks between Rio and Nicky.

“Neighbours?” Rio asks confused. “Agatha, it’s me, it’s us,” Rio says to her, getting a horrible feeling deep inside.

“I’m sorry you must have me confused for someone else, I’m Agnes,” Agnes says, looking at Rio with something that she realises is worse than the hate she was expecting, a look of complete unfamiliarity.

“No, I know exactly who you are,” Rio says, taking a step towards her. “Agatha, I know you know me, look deep inside of yourself, what we have is stronger than whatever is going on with you,” Rio says. “Please, I’m your wife, your Rio,“  Rio says, and for a split second Rio thinks she sees a look of a recognition in Agatha’s eyes, but it quickly disappears.

“I don’t know who…” Agnes says, clearly confused, as she tries to move back, clearly becoming overwhelmed with whatever is going on with her.

“I’m yours,” Rio says, reaching out to Agnes and as she does, she flinches away.

“Mom stop,” Nicky suddenly says, taking a step forward. “She’s under a spell,” Nicky reveals. “I can feel it,” Nicky says, squinting his eyes at Agatha as he tries to ‘see’ it in a sense.

“Magic’s not real,” Agnes says, and those words being said by Agatha disturbs Rio more than she would admit.

“What does it feel like?” Rio asks Nicky, ignoring Agnes for the moment, as she realises that Agatha doesn’t have the answers she needs, Nicky does.

“Like a spider, crawling all through her, getting into every part of her,” Nicky admits, shivering as it feels completely wrong to him, which is why he isn’t sure that is the best explanation, but it is the one he is giving. “And it’s going deeper with everything you say,” Nicky tells his mother.

“We have to break it,” Rio says, knowing that they cannot leave Agatha in this state.

“I… I don’t know if I can be, I’ve never felt magic like this… it’s chaos,” Nicky admits, trying to make sense of what he is feeling.

“Chaos magic,” Rio mutters, knowing that sounds familiar, and it quickly comes to her as to why. “The Scarlett Witch,” Rio realises, knowing from what Agatha once told her how bad that is. “You talk to her, try to break through,” Rio tells Nicky.

“What if I make it worse?” Nicky asks worried.

“It can’t get worse than this,” Rio admits, as while she was prepared for hatred, prepared to have Agatha once more say that she never wants to see her again, what she wasn’t prepared for is Agatha just not knowing them.

“Okay,” Nicky says. “Mama?” Nicky asks, hesitantly, “It’s me, Nicky, Mom saved me, she brought me back, and I’ve missed you so much,” Nicky says, desperately hoping that the connection they share will be enough to get through and at first, it’s almost like it did.

“Nicky,” Agatha says amazed, tears coming to her eyes. “Rio,” Agatha says, looking at her with love and affection, and for a second everything seems like it is going to be okay.

“NO!” Nicky suddenly yells, as he feels the spell Agatha is under get stronger, draw more strength from the witch who cast it, he feels it almost strangling Agatha which causes her eye to roll back into her head and for her to collapse, but as Rio is able to move so quickly, she is able to get to Agatha before she can hit the ground. “I’m sorry!” Nicky exclaims, feeling horrified at what he did. “I’m sorry!” Nicky says, blaming himself for what just happened.

“Nicky, it’s okay, help me get her inside,” Rio says to her son as while she could carry Agatha alone without a problem, it’s something she has done before without a problem, after what just happened, she knows that Nicky needs to do something to help, and together both Nicky and Rio carry Agatha into the house. “Let’s get her to the couch,” Rio suggests, noticing that the house is very unlike Agatha.

“This is worse, this is so much worse!” Nicky exclaims as he and Rio gently lay Agatha on the couch.

“She’s alive,” Rio says to Nicky, after physically checking that, not just trusting her magic. “We’ll figure this out,” Rio assures her son, turning away from Agatha for the moment to look at Nicky, needing to believe that.

“I don’t know if we can, Mom,” Nicky admits. “I felt it, she was remembering us, she knew, and the spell got stronger. She lost conscious because the strength of the spell was fighting against how connected she is to us,” Nicky admits.

“Which means she is still in there, we just have to get to her,” Rio tells Nicky.

“How? We tried and she collapsed,” Nicky reminds her. “I can feel the spell getting stronger, the magic…. its bonding itself to her… how do we get rid of that?” Nicky asks, feeling lost as he doesn’t see how they are going to do it.

“By trusting that our bond is stronger,” Rio tells Nicky. “Because it is,” Rio says.

“Is it? She remembered us for a second and she collapsed,” Nicky says worried.

“That’s exactly my point, I’ve been fighting for Agatha for over three hundred years, I’m not going to stop now, and you can’t either,” Rio tells her son.

“Okay,” Nicky says with a nod, though he still doesn’t understand how they are going to reverse this. “How do we get her back?” Nicky asks.

“We need to understand the spell, understand exactly what happened here,” Rio says, as she looks around her. “Until we understand a bit more, we can’t risk trying to break the spell again, we can’t risk it getting stronger,” Rio admits, getting a feeling that it is already going to be hard enough to break the spell so they can’t make it any harder.

“We can’t abandon her to it,” Nicky objects, as while he is terrified of making things worse, he knows they can’t do that.

“We won’t, we’ll never leave her, Nicky,” Rio promises, and as she does Nicky sees something.

“Señor Scratchy?” Nicky asks amazed as he sees a rabbit who he walks over to. “It’s you, isn’t it? it’s really you,” Nicky says, as he picks up and cuddles with the rabbit he loved so dearly before he died. “How’s this possible?” Nicky asks, looking at Rio.

“It’s easy to make certain animals immortal,” Rio explains, knowing that even though not many witches have tried. “Mama must not have wanted to say goodbye to him,” Rio says, smiling slightly as she knows that is just the kind of sentimental thing Agatha would deny ever doing.

“I’m glad, you’ve been looking after Mama, right?” Nicky asks, as he continues to pet his pet rabbit while Rio sits down next to Agatha. “Been with her when I couldn’t be?”

“I don’t know what happened to you, who you pissed off, but I’ll figure it out,” Rio says to Agatha, keeping her voice so low that Nicky doesn’t hear. “We’ll get you back, no matter what it takes,” Rio promises.

About an hour later Nicky and Rio are still in Agnes’s house with Agatha, who is still unconscious. While Rio is sitting next to Agatha Nicky has been doing some exploring, trying to get some answers about what is going on.

“There is nothing magical here, no spell books, no runes, nothing,” Nicky admits as he walks back into the living room.

“That’s probably because of the spell,” Rio assumes, knowing that the mere fact that the Darkhold is gone says a lot, and as she does, she starts to see the signs that tell her that Agatha is waking up, as after spending centuries watching Agatha sleep, she can always tell when she is about to wake up. “Nicky, go wait outside,” Rio tells her son.

“Why?” Nicky asks confused.

“Because you don’t need to do this again,” Rio tells her son, being sure that once again being around Agatha who doesn’t remember him is just going to hurt Nicky. “Go,” Rio says, and Nicky, reluctantly heads out of the room, getting out of the room just as Agatha wakes up.

“Who…” Agnes starts to say, when she opens her eyes and sees Rio sitting right next to her, leaning over her, clearly confused.

“I’m your new neighbour,” Rio answers, as it is the first explanation she can think to give. “I saw you fall while gardening, I think you must have gotten too hot,” Rio explains, it being the first explanation she can think to give, it feeling completely wrong to lie to Agatha as it’s not something she has ever done before.

“And you helped me,” Agnes explains to Rio, who is smirking slightly, a smirk which Rio usually just enjoyed seeing but now just reminds her of what is missing.

“I was around,” Rio says, feeling a little uncomfortable, as while the person before he might look like her Agatha, she isn’t actually her Agatha. “Um, so I should go,” Rio says, as she stands up.

“You don’t have to,” Agnes says. “I feel like I owe you a drink,” Agnes says, as she pushes herself up so she is siting up.

“Raincheck,” Rio says, as this is far from the reaction she was expecting because it’s not actually Agatha it feels wrong to take her up for the offer of a drink, and what she is sure will happen after that. “I’m really glad you’re okay,” Rio says, feeling suffocated, like she cannot be around this version of Agatha for much longer. “Te Veo,” Rio says, before turning around and leaving, fighting back tears as she goes.

Once she is out of Agatha’s sight Rio wipes away her teers, takes several deep breaths to pull herself together, then heads out of the house, even though ever part of herself tells her to turn back around and make Agatha remember, no matter what it takes.

“Mom?” Nicky asks, once Rio is outside, and as he sees the look on his mother’s face, the look she is desperately trying to hide, Nicky walks up to her and hugs his mother tightly.

As mother and son stand on the step together, taking comfort from each other as they both feel heartbroken, so close to the person they have spent five years searching for, but feeling even further from her than they felt when they had no idea where she was.
