“Yeah,” Alice confirms.

“Mrs Hart,” Jen says to her.

“It’s Sharon,”

“Sharon, you are so pretty,” Jen tells her.

“Thank you,”

“But since you were the first to drink, you’re our canary in a coal mine,” Jen advises.

“Okay,” Sharon says, and she goes to take another drink but Nicky quickly, without even thinking about it, reaches out and stops her. The second Nicky touches Sharon what he has been sensing is confirmed, and he knows that she is going to die soon, and there is nothing that can be done to change that.

“No, it’s poisoned Sharon, remember,” Nicky says to her, his voice stuttering, taking the glass, even though he knows her fate is sealed, but considering he isn’t sensing anything about anyone else he has to assume that not everyone dies.

“Why don’t you just let her drink it all,” Agatha says, causing everyone to look at her, which gives Nicky a few seconds to pull himself together, as he knows there is no point telling anyone what he can tell about Sharon’s fate as there is nothing that can change it, but considering he isn’t feeling anything from anyone else he suspects they still have a chance to complete the trial.

“Uh, it serves our best interest is all,” Agatha says, using her hair to hide the fact that she hasn’t drunk the wine, and therefore isn’t experiencing symptoms.

“Okay, I’m gonna ask you a few questions so we can try to identity the toxin, okay?” Jen asks, turning to look at Sharon. “Do you feel a tingling in the back of your throat?” Jen asks, and as she asks her questions Agatha searches for another way out.

“No,”

“Do you taste mulberries?” Jen asks.

“What do mulberries taste like?” Sharon asks confused.

“Do you hear any ringing or the sound of fairies crying?” Jen asks.

“Huh?” Sharon asks confused.

“I love you guys,” Lilia suddenly says, to everyone’s confusion.

“My hearts racing,” Alice says.

“That’s another one,” Jen says. “Also, hallucinations, and eventually… Death,” Jen says, looking at Agatha, and just like his mama the second Jen mentions death Nicky doesn’t think about the concept of death he thinks of his mom, the personification of death, and while he wants to see her Agatha really doesn’t right now.

“How do you spell, Alewife?” Nicky asks, wanting to write that down, as he wants to understand as much as possible.

“I gotta get out of here,” Agatha says, running to the doors and trying to use a candlestick to break open the windows. Something which is not working. While everyone else is just confused by her behaviour Nicky is surprised because he realises that his mama would be acting the way she is because she doesn’t want to see Rio when she comes to collect anyone who dies.

“What are you doing?” Lilia asks surprised.

“She’s gone crazy,” Sharon says.

“You can’t run from the poison,” Jen tells Agatha, and as she does Nicky realises something.

“Agatha didn’t drink the poison,” Nicky says, picking up his mama’s full glass and carrying it over to the others.  “You can’t cheat, Agatha,” Nicky says, though considering everything his mom told him he would imagine Agatha is seeing this more as doing what she has to do to survive rather than cheating.

“Why? Who says?” Agatha asks.

“The road,” Jen says.

“Oh, that’s ridiculous! We don’t all have to suffer,” Agatha argues. “Teen didn’t drink,” Agatha points out, giving Nicky an idea of just what he may have to try.

“He’s not in the oven. And he’s underage!” Jen exclaims, and considering when he was actually born Nicky can’t help but wonder if that is actually technically true.

“I’m gonna shove it down your gullet, so help me…” Lila says, and Agatha takes the glass from Nicky and smashes it.

“No!”

“On the upholstery?” Sharon asks.

“We’re wasting time!” Jen argues.

“You have to drink Agatha,” Alice tells her.

“Well, I would, but there is no more wine, so…” Agatha starts to say, and Alice picks up one of the empty glasses and as she holds it, it fills up with wine. “So cute,” Agatha says, moving backwards from the glass.

“No!” Agatha exclaims, knowing she cannot let Nicky, even if she doesn’t know he is Nicky, drink poison, and she pushes Nicky back and takes the glass from Alice, which she drinks in one go. “Augh, it’s so cheap,” Agatha says, pulling a face as she finishes the wine.

“Please, please, Wanda? Wanda, I’m begging you. Let him breathe, please,” Sharon begs, and as she does Nicky notices the almost disturbed look on his mamas face.

“So, those hallucinations seem chill,” Nicky comments, feeling worried about what is going to do to everyone, especially his mama.

Over the next little while, while Jen is getting everything ready in the kitchen, everyone else, with the exception of Sharon who is unconscious, is searching for the other ingredients that Jen needs to complete the potion. Having been partnered with Alice, who just had a hallucination, Nicky is with her heading back to the kitchen, and when they to the main area of the house they find Jen, who from the look of her, clearly just had a hallucination too.

“You okay?” Alice asks Jen.

“That’s just a gross term for honey, isn’t it?” Nicky asks, as that is what he assumes.

“Salt water,” Jen confirms.

Once Sharon is lying on the table everyone else, carrying the ingredients they collected, hurry over to the sink where Jen is brewing the potion.

“Okay, the elements need to be added in a certain order, in a specific time, starting with gut and eye,” Jen instructs.

“I knew it,” Agatha says, feeling rather smug about that, as she and Lilia add everything they have collected into the potion.

“Obliviously. Yes, three drops,” Jen says.

“Take your time,” Jen says annoyed.

“Let me help,” Nicky says, taking the bottle from Alice, and as he does his hand brushes her and he feels nothing which tells him she is a certainty to die soon, which makes him feel a little better. “One, two, three,” Nicky says, as he adds each of the drops into the potion.

“It’s working, it’s working right?” Agatha asks as the potion changes colour.

“Huh,” Jen says as she stares at the potion.

“In the middle of a traumatic hallucination. No, Agatha, I did not!” Jen exclaims, and as she does Nicky gets an idea.

“Is there a sous vide?” Nicky asks.

“Oh brilliant,” Jen says, as Lilia and Agatha look confused, and Nicky quickly hurries to search for one.

“That’s something people know about?” Agatha asks, looking at Lila, who looks just as confused, having no idea what that is.

“It’s a super fancy cooking tool,” Nicky explains, finding it and hurrying back over to the seat with it. “It heats water to a specific temperature, so that you can cook your meat easily,” Nicky says as he puts it in the water and plugs it in. “I love using mine,” Nicky reveals, as his mom got him one a few months back.

“Ah cute,” Agatha says to him, though she files ‘loves to cook’ away on the list she is keeping about him.

“TEEN!” Jen yells as she can’t pick up a wooden spoon so Nicky quicky gets it for her, before hurrying back to the sink.

“I need you to stir with your dominant hand, counterclockwise,” Jen instructs, and Nicky quickly starts to do that without a problem. “Everyone, pull a strand of hair outta your head now,” Jen tells everyone and as she starts to give instructs Agatha suddenly sees a bassinet appears and a baby crying.

Hurrying over to the bassinet Agatha quickly moves the blanket and to her absolute horror she doesn’t see her baby, her little boy, she sees the Darkhold, and she moves back in horror and devastation.

“Agatha!” Jen says, trying to snap her back to reality.

“What did you see?” Nicky asks his mama concerned, suspecting that what she saw has to do with him, or if not him then his mom.

“Nothing,” Agatha says, even though she is so far from okay.

“Agatha, we need your hair,” Jen tells Agatha, and she, despite still feeling haunted by what she just saw, gets back to her feet, pulls her hair and gets to the sink.

“Okay, wait, now,” Jen says and once she does Jen, Agatha, Alice and Lilia all drop their hair into the potion.

“Stop stirring,” Jen tells Nicky who does just that. “We need to clasp hands,” Jen says, and everyone does that. As Nicky claps hands with both Lilia and Jen Nicky feels nothing that tells them they are going to die soon which means the only person he hasn’t confirmed is going to be okay, as touch is the only way for him to be completely certain, is the one person he wants to know about most, his mama. “And clear your minds. Once are intensions are aligned, it will glow bright cerulean,” Jen reveals.

“What are our intentions again?” Agatha asks.

“To not die,” Jen tells her in an annoyed tone of voice.

“I get cerulean and chartreuse confused. Is cerulean the green one?” Alice, who has opened her eyes, asks.

“No, it’s blue,” Jen says.

“Then it’s not workin,” Alice reveals, causing the others to open their eyes.

“It’s like a blue green, maybe like a teal?” Nicky suggests.

“It’s green, Teen,” Lilia tells him.

“Something is wrong. I must have forgotten something,” Jen says, becoming upset.

“One minute left,” Alice, who is looking at the timer, says.

“What did you forget?” Agatha asks Jen.

“I don’t know!” Jen exclaims. “I’ve never made this potion before! I make retinol serums, for Christ sake!” Jen exclaims.

“Fifty seconds,” Alice says.

“There was a time where I would be able to just solve this with a wave of my hand, but now?” Jen asks, becoming upset. “I’m bound. He stole my magic!” Jen exclaims, becoming even more upset. “We’re all going to die here,” Jen says, moving back from everyone. “I don’t want to die here,” Jen says, and before Nicky can test to see if the Sigil will let him assure Jen that she isn’t going to die during this trial, his Mama beats him to it.

“I have always hated you,” Agatha says as she puts both her hands on Jen’s shoulders, trying to get her to focus.

“If this is a pep talk…” Jen starts to say, having no idea what Agatha is doing.

“But I left you alone because what you were doing is important,” Agatha tells Jen. “Not this Kale Care crap, the real work,” Agatha says, as she knows how incredible the way Jen helps women, especially pregnant women, is. “You can be that witch again,” Agatha says to Jen, that being the nicest thing Agatha has ever said to her. “They can take your power, Jen, but they can’t take your knowledge,” Agatha says, as she always feels that knowledge is incredibly important. “Jen?” Agatha asks, needing her to have the answer already.

“Blood,” Jen suddenly says.

“Whose and how much?” Agatha asks.

“We need the blood of the poisoned,” Jen reveals, and while he knows that means him Nicky is a little worried that his blood, considering who he is the son off, won’t have the desired effect, but he can’t raise his concerns due to the sigil.

“Thirty seconds,” Alice says as Agatha grabs the knife.

“Thanks for being underage,” Agatha says before cutting Nicky’s hand, and as she does that Nicky uses the opportunity to touch her hand, without Agatha realising, and as he does, he is reassured when he doesn’t experience the sensation that tells him she is going to die with no possible way of surviving, because it means his mama is going to survive, this trial at least.

After Nicky’s blood drops into the potion, it takes a few second before it changes colour and Agatha, Alice, Jen and Lila all drink, all of them immediately feeling the antidote working.

“The timer’s still ticking!” Jen exclaims.

“Mrs Hart,” Nicky says, even though he knows it will be no use, and the group passes the antidote between them until it is poured into her mouth, and at the exact same second the potion is poured into her mouth the timer stops and the oven, clearly their exit, opens.

“Is that our exit?” Alice asks surprised.

“I am not climbing in an oven,” Lilia objects. “That happened to a friend of mine, she had a lovely house, and she ended up…” Lilia starts to say but before she can give more of a explanation everyone screams as water bursts into the room.

“Move it,” Jen says, and she pushes everyone else out of the way to exit through the oven, and after Jen exits Llia does.

“Help me with her!” Alice says, referring to Sharon.

“Not a chance,” Agatha argues.

“We don’t know what happens if we leave her behind,” Nicky says as while he can tell Sharon is certainly going to die, he can tell that she hasn’t died yet.

“Fine!” Agatha says with a scoff, and with something difficulty she, Nicky, and Alice manage to get her through the oven, and after they do Nicky goes next.

As soon as he is through the exit Nicky goes straight to Sharon, who he knows is barely hanging on.

“It’s okay,” Nicky says reassuringly to Sharon, his voice too quiet for anyone else to hear. “You’re going to see someone familiar really soon and she’s going to take you to where you need to go,” Nicky tells Sharon, though with the Sigil he isn’t even sure if Sharon will recognize Rio, even after her death.  “You don’t have to be afraid, it will be okay,” Nicky assures Sharon, taking her hand, wanting to give her some comfort in her last moments.

“Ouch…” Sharon says, moaning, clearly in pain and as he takes her hand Nicky can feel that she is going to experiencing a few minutes of incredibly pain before dying, and there is nothing he can do to change her ultimate fate, but what he can do is take away the pain she is feeling.

“It’s okay. You’ll be okay, you’ll be in a better place, trust me, I’ve been there, it’s okay,” Nicky says, and he does something incredibly painful, he uses a small amount of his magic to end her suffering by squeezing her lungs so she can’t breathe, ending her life in seconds rather than the several painful minutes she was going to experience. “I’m sorry,” Nicky says, feeling extremely guilty, but also feeling like he did the right thing because he knows there was nothing that would have saved her.

Having no idea what Nicky just did, Agatha is pushing everyone else out of the way as she walks down the ‘slide’ they just used to come out of the trial.

“A little rusty there, Jen?” Agatha asks her.

“A little traitorous there, Agatha?” Jen responds.

“Stop,” Lilia tells them, knowing that the last thing they need right now is for Agatha and Jen to start fighting again. “We’re alive. We made it through the first test. Everyone is safe,” Lilia says.

“Nott everyone,” Nicky says. “Sharon’s dead,” Nicky reveals, closing her eyes, and hoping that she is already with his mom on her way to where she needs to go a place where she won’t be in the pain she was just in.

“Who’s Sharon?” Agatha asks.

Chapter 21

Chapter 21

AN: This is a shorter chapter, but the next ones will more than make up for it. I promise. Because of that (and the fact that I have the next two days off work) I will update the next chapter a little sooner in like 9ish hours. Thank you so much for the incredible response to the last chapter. It means so much to me.

Moments after Nicky tells everyone that Sharon is dead, he gets started on digging her grave as he feels that because he sped up her death, even if it was for the right reasons, the least he can do is make sure she is laid to rest properly.

As he digs the grave Nicky, who is doing his best not to think about what he did as while he feels like it was the right thing he still feels guilty, notices his mama inspecting Sharon’s body and he really hopes she hasn’t realised what he did, as he doesn’t want to let her down. Unknown to Nicky Agatha has realised that Sharon was killed by magic even if she doesn’t know the full story.

“I didn’t think you had it in you,” Agatha says, suspecting she knows exactly who aided Sharon in her demise, even though she can’t tell for sure, and she knows that if she is right then it is certainly a surprised.

“You didn’t think who had what in them?” Nicky asks his mama, hoping she hasn’t realised what he did as there is no way for him to explain why he did it when the Sigil is in place, and he really wants to explain himself. Hearing Nicky’s question Agatha just winks at him, making it clear that she isn’t going to tell anyone what she has realised, and allowing Nicky to believe, just for a moment, that she won’t be disappointed in him once the Sigil is broken.

For the next few minutes Nicky continues to dig Sharons’ grave, getting some help from Alice, who doesn’t want to talk to Jen and Lila anymore, while Lilia and Jen sit down on rocks, and Agatha, who has taken her hair down, uses a tree to stretch.

“Uh, RIP, Mrs Hart,” Agatha suddenly says, causing everyone but Nicky to look at her. “Well, shall we?” Agatha asks, wanting to get going before Rio turns up, as Agatha is sure she will, but to her annoyance nobody makes an effort to move. “Okay, so what’s the problem now?” Agatha asks, looking between the others.

“A woman is dead, Agatha,” Lilia says, in a ‘why do I have to point out the obvious’ tone of voice.

“Yes, and Alice and Teen are kindly digging a grave for her,” Agatha says, pointing to where Nicky and Agatha are almost finished burying Mrs Hart. “So, they’ll catch up when they can Vamonos,” Agatha says, slipping into Spanish without even thinking about it, trying to avoid being around when Rio shows up to collect Mrs Hart, and she dramatic flares her coat, but once again no one follows her. “Okay, Mrs Hart was a bad draft pick, okay? Of course, the road killed her,” Agatha says, even though she almost positive Nicky played a part in Sharon’s death, she doesn’t plan on telling anyone that. “More power for the rest of us,” Agatha says, rubbing her hands in an excited way.

“Setting aside your staggering callousness,” Jen says, standing up. “We still have the issue of our incomplete Coven,” Jen points out.

“Oh. Okay. Yes. Okay, now I know the confusion,” Agatha says, understanding what Jen is thinking. “We needed the whole gang to access the Road, but after that it’s anybody’s game,” Agatha reveals. “It’s like the Ballard says, ‘Burn and brew with coven two, and glory shall be thine,” Agatha miss-quotes with a chuckle.

“The Ballard clearly says with cover TRUE, glory shall be thine,” Jen corrects, giving Agatha an annoyed look.

“Does it?” Agatha asks with a laugh. “It’s coven two!” Agatha exclaims.

“That doesn’t make any sense,” Jen argues, the annoyance she is feeling towards Agatha being perfectly clear in her voice.

“Does if you’re a student of the Ballard,” Agatha responds, becoming even more annoyed by Jen like she constantly is.

“Her mother recorded the most popular version of the ballad,” Lilia says, trying to put an end to the fight that is going on. “So maybe we ask Alice,” Lilia suggests.

“How many witches left the Road with you last time?” Alice asks Agatha, as Nicky puts flowers down on Sharon’s grave, muttering another apology as he does, and Agatha puts up one finger as she the only person who left The Road with her last time was Rio, and she’s a lot more than a witch.

“Well, whatever,” Jen says with a shrug. “We still need a Green Witch. We would not have survived the last trial without my expertise,” Jen argues.

“Not all of us did,” Alice points out.

“Well, where were you when Mrs Hart needed protection?” Jen argues, and Agatha is clearly becoming amused with all the bickering, but she also keeps glancing over at Nicky who is staring at Sharon’s grave, not really noticing what the others are doing as he is still thinking about what he did.

“According to my count, Mrs Hart drank two glasses of the poisoned wine,” Lilia says. “How many doses of the antidote did she get, Potions witch?” Lilia asks. “This is our fault,” Lilia says.

“Okay, wow,” Jen says, clearly insulted.

“Ohh,” Agatha comments, becoming more interested, in the debate that is going on.

“It’s everyone’s fault!” Nicky says, as he stands up and walks over to them, knowing it was his fault her death happened sooner, but it was going to happen anyway and that is on everyone. “We were supposed to look out for each other, but we didn’t,” Nicky tells the others. “That was our fatal mistake,” Nicky says, remembering what his mom said about death coming easy on the Road, and realising that she was right, and he hates that he had to feel it coming for Sharon, knowing that there was nothing he could do, that he was completely powerless.

“Most fatal for Mrs Hart,” Agatha trying to lightly the mood a little.

“I feel like we should go back,” Nicky says, looking upset, as while he knows he has to finish the road to save his family, he doesn’t want to experience knowing someone else he is with is going to die before they do again, something which he knows will be hard to ignore if they continue to be so close to each other.

“We can’t,” Alice tells him in a gentle voice. “We can’t go back, and we shouldn’t go forward. Not without a replacement Green Witch,” Alice comments.

“People can’t be replaced,” Nicky says, and as he does Agatha gets an idea.

“Can’t they?” Agatha asks, knowing what they can do, and having a sinking suspicion that she knows exactly who it will summon, but she just hopes she is wrong and because of that she is trying hard not to think about her suspicion. “What if we summon a backup green witch?” Agatha asks, and like his mama Nicky suspects he knows exactly who will be called, but unlike his mama he hopes his suspicion is correct as even if she doesn’t know who he is he really, really, wants to see her again, especially considering what he just did.

“To the Road?” Jen asks shocked.

“There is so much that can go wrong,” Alice says horrified, feeling that there is no way this could end well.

“So much has already gone wrong,” Agatha points out, and Nicky agrees with her about that. “I mean, aren’t we already coven-less witches, and by extension, rule breakers, right?” Agatha asks, looking between Lilia, Jen and Alice as they are the ones who she has to convince.

“I guess, we just have to be careful, and specific, but mostly careful,” Lilia comments, feeling that it could work.

“Yes, well said,” Agatha says approvingly, and she knows that now Lilia has agreed the others will, something which is confirmed when Alice nods and Jen shrugs.

“Now, anyone have a spell book?” Lilia asks, and everyone turns to Nicky who nods and pulls his spell book out his pocket, being careful not to accidently pull his knife as he does, because he knows he can’t answer the questions that will cause if anyone, his mama especially, sees it, and once he has the book, he hands it to his mama.

Over the next few minutes Agatha, Alice, Jen, and Lilia, mainly Agatha and Lilia who have clearly done something like this before, set up what they need for the spell, and as they do Nicky becomes pretty sure that it’s going to be his mom that they summon, and he can’t wait to see how his mama reacts to that.

Once everything is set up the group stands in a line, Nicky standing right next to his mama, Agatha starts to chant in Latin and wave her hand over the silhouette of a person that they have made out of dirt and leaves.

“May she be strong and wise, and the best at her craft,” Lilia says, as she puts a crystal down on the silhouette.

“May she be smart, and not annoying,” Agatha says as she puts a flower down on the silhouette. “And also, not super political,” Agatha adds before standing up.

“May she be pleasant looking,” Jen says, also putting her object down.

“Can she bring some Advil?” Alice asks as she puts her object down, causing Lilia to scoff.

“Yeah, okay,” Agatha says and once Alice puts down her object Agatha casts the rest of the incantation, hands Nicky back his spell book, and waves her hand three times, as the wind picks up.

“Now what?” Nicky asks, looking at his mama for the answer, but it is not her who answers, it’s Lilia.

“Now we wait,” Lilia explains. “True witchcraft takes time. The spell must marinate, gestate,” Lilia advises, and as soon as she says the words there is the sound of someone crawling out of the grave, they made for Sharon causing everyone to scream and gasp as they turn to see what is going on.

“Agatha, what did you do?” Jen yells, as Agatha tries to push everyone back from, who Nicky knows to be, his mom.

“What do you mean, what did I do? This was clearly a group effort,” Agatha says, not understanding why she is getting blamed for something they all did.

“Did we create a zombie? What spell did we cast?” Alice asks as she takes Nicky’s spell book and tries to search it to figure out what they just did.

“Why is the print so small?” Lilia asks annoyed, as she cannot make out what is on the pages.

“Hi, are you okay?” Nicky asks, causing Agatha to be suspicious why he isn’t more freaked out, as while he knows it’s his mom she is clearly still adjusting to being on The Road and what had to happen to get her there. As it becomes clear who it is Nicky desperately wants to run to her, hug her, and confess what he did, but because he knows he can’t he looks at his mama to distract himself by seeing how she reacts.

“Heard you were having a party,” Rio says, in a very casual way, like she didn’t just craw out of a grave.

“How did you…” Agatha says, looking at Rio with an annoyed look on her face, as while she suspected Rio would be the one who came she had hoped that her suspicion was wrong.

“I was in the neighbourhood,” Rio says with a smirk, both Agatha and Nicky knowing exactly why that was, as she moves closer to Agatha. “Surprise, M’Lady,” Rio says, presenting Agatha with the same flower Agatha put down to cast the spell, and while Nicky is amused that her mom is flirting considering everything, Agatha looks furious and goes to attack her, but both Jen and Alice grab her arm, trying to keep her from Rio.

“We just summoned her,” Jen reminds Agatha.

“What need her, what are you doing?” Alice asks confused, as Rio just grins, not at all phased by Agatha’s behaviour as she was expecting it.

Letting out an annoyed yell Agatha pulls herself free from the others and walks away. As he sees his mama walk away Nicky looks between his mama and mom and for a second, he debates what to do, but then he decides to follow his mama as he figures it will be the better option as his mom is likely just going to introduce herself to the others as her ‘The Green Witch’ identity, where his Mama doesn’t seem completely okay.

“Agatha wait!” Nicky calls after his Mama as he hurries to catch up with her, but she is walking surprisingly fast, which requires him to run fast until he finally catches up with her. “So, the dangerous-but charismatic lady is back,” Nicky says, it feeling very odd to describe his mother like that, but as he isn’t meant to know exactly who he is there is nothing else he can say, at least nothing that won’t trigger the Sigil, and he isn’t overly surprised when his mama groans in response to that. “Do you wanna talk about it?” Nicky asks, and he isn’t overly surprised when his mama ignores the question. “Are we in trouble, Agatha? Like more than we were ten minutes ago?” Nicky asks, and Agatha ignores that question too, so they just continue to walk.

As Agatha continues to walk with Nicky by her side, and the others catching up behind, she can’t help but think about Nicky’s question. Technically she knows the rest of the Coven aren’t in trouble, that Rio can’t hurt them or do anything to them, but she knows she is, because Rio has power over her that has nothing to do with her identity of Death or even The Green Witch; power that no one else has.

Whenever Agatha is around Rio, she remembers how much love she has for the eternal being, she remembers how Rio was the first being who made her feel safe, like she wasn’t evil, who made her feel like a woman, who made her feel like it was okay to feel period, and whenever she is around her, she remembers that, and the family they created out of that love. But, along with all the good things she remembers about Rio whenever they are near each other, she also remembers the bad. She remembers the pain, grief, anger, and betrayal she felt when Rio took their son, the very thing that led her to the Darkhold, to Wanda, to spending three years under another’s control, something she long ago swore she would never let happen again.

“Agatha,” Nicky says hesitantly, cutting through Agatha’s thoughts, and she looks at him. “If you do want to talk about it, I’m here,” Nicky tells his mama as they continue to walk, Agatha once again ignoring his statement, but she does find it extremely interesting that he said it.

For a little while the group continue to walk, Nicky being sure that Alice, Lilia, and Jen are both intrigued and terrified of his mom, something which he knows is a pretty standard reaction, while Rio herself is clearly having fun, and Agatha is doing her best to ignore Rio, not talking to anyone else in the process. As he is becoming rather uncomfortable with both his moms being so quiet, and he wants to help them, Nicky is desperately searching his mind for something to say when he notices something in the distance.

“Here we go, again,” Nicky says, noticing the house they are walking towards.

“Pass,” Alice says, turning to walk in the other direction, clearly not wanting to go into the house as she has a feeling that it is going to be her trial.

“A mutiny already?” Rio asks Agatha, with an amused look on her face, and Agatha ignores her as she hurries to catch up with Alice.

“Alice? Alice?” Agatha asks as she hurries to catch up with Alice. “What’s the plan, Alice?” Agatha asks, as she gets to Alice’s side.

“Go back, go around, go anywhere but in that house,” Alice says and as soon as she says that they see that the house that leads to the next trial is now in front of them instead of behind them.

“Um, I agree, but the road clearly doesn’t,” Agatha comments. “So, I guess we go,” Agatha says, and the group continue to walk until they get to the house that is clearly red and just like the last house there is a large moon on the door.

“Waxing moon,” Agatha realises, as she takes note of the image.

“The Fire phase,” Nicky says, his mama nods, and one by one the group head into the house, Alice doing so hesitantly, where they will find the second trial. As they walk in Nicky finds a way to subtly touch everyone but his mom, who he knows can’t die, and to his relief he doesn’t feel anything that tells him that any of them are certainly going to die soon.

As soon as everyone walk into the second trial everyone is once again changed, this time into seventies attire, very much looking like a rock group.

“Don’t drink anything. Don’t eat anything. Don’t touch anything,” Alice warns.

“The Road isn’t subtle,” Alice comments, knowing that she looks a lot like her mother and her band.

“Knock, knock.” Rio says, walking into the room from the opposite door to the one Agatha used to walk in, not giving Agatha even a moment of piece. “How’s the quest for power going?” Rio asks curious, as she walks close to Agatha.

“It’s going,” Agatha responds, closing her vest a little.

“Oh, they’re my new best friends!” Agatha says, putting on an excited voice.

“Hmm,” Agatha says, not overly surprised that Rio was called, but still not overly happy, as Rio looks out of the window.

“Why did you bring that boy?” Rio asks, pointing at Nicky as from her current perspective he is a mystery boy as for the first time, ever, she cannot tell who he is. The mere fact that she can’t tell who he is makes her extremely curious and she can’t help but wonder Agatha knows about the fact that, who seems like a random kid to her, is so completely hidden, even from her.

“Oh, many hands,” Agatha says, moving quickly to Rio as she doesn’t want Rio to focus on Nicky until she has more concrete evidence about who he is, because if she is wrong it is going to be painful enough for her, she doesn’t want that for Rio too. “Maybe The Road is like Switzerland,” Agatha says to Rio as she moves closer to her, not having the energy to keep fighting with Rio, and the truth is, not that she would admit it, she doesn’t want to. “What if we just call a truce?” Agatha asks. “Just... I don’t know. Just one more big adventure,” Agatha suggests, knowing that they have had a lot of adventures together, most of which are some of her favourite memories. “You and me,” Agatha says, as she feels Rio moving her finger around on her thigh, something which they both know Agatha loves.

“Like old times?” Rio asks hopefully, as even without her memories of Nicky being alive that’s what she wants most, for her and Agatha to go back to what they once were.

“Work and play,” Agatha confirms, knowing that Rio would be thinking about the same thing she is. “It could be nice, right?” Agatha asks, and Rio is sure it would be a lot more than just ‘nice’. “I just need these witches to get me to the end,” Agatha explains. “So, you tell me, what happens next,” Agatha says, subtly reaching out and pressing the intercom so that the others can hear Rio’s answer, as just because she isn’t going to tell them who Rio is doesn’t mean she can’t have Rio give them hints that will lead to them figuring it out on their own.

“I get the pleasure of watching you do what you do best,” Rio says, her voice playing throughout the other room, causing Nicky to wonder what the hell his moms are talking about, though he suspects he doesn’t want to know.

“Which is?” Agatha asks, in a seductive voice.

“Kill all the witches around you, one by one,” Rio says, and as she does Nicky notices the others exchange shocked looks.

“Then what?” Agatha asks.

“You get your power, and I get my bodies,” Rio says, Nicky being the only person other than Agatha who knows what that means.

“Hey! That’s my coven you’re talking about,” Agatha says, in an over the top insulted voice. “I’m not that kind of witch anymore,” Agatha says, as Rio laughs, very much feeling amused with Agatha’s shenanigans, just like she always has.

“I knew it!” Jen yells and as the others start to yell various things as they head closer to the others Nicky notices a record with ‘play me’ on it, and even though he knows it could be dangerous he also knows it’s likely a clue, but he also figures that it’s probably a good idea to distract everyone from what his moms just said, and because of that he plays the record.

The second the record starts to play there is a shriek from the record and everyone, except for Rio, have to grab their ears in pain.

“What is that?” Jen asks, as Agatha and Rio hurry out of the sound booth.

“I’m sorry, I thought it was a clue,” Nicky admits, as he did truly think that, even if he was also trying to distract everyone from his moms.

“What makes you think that?” Alice asks, and as she does Agatha realises something.

“It’s spinning backwards,” Agatha says, and once she does a demonic voice starts to speak indistinctly which causes everyone to scream.

“Make it stop!” Jen yells.

“Stop it. turn it off!” Alice yells.

As the others yell, clutching their ears, Agatha hurries towards the record player which she picks up and throws to the ground, breaking the play and the record; stopping the sound.

“We’ve been cursed,” Lilia realises as the metronome starts to tick, telling everyone that the trial has started.

“I think that means the trial started,” Rio says amused.

“Why are you smiling?” Jen asks confused, not understanding Rio at all.

“She’s a tourist,” Agatha says, deciding not to explain more than that as any other explanation will lead to way too many questions she doesn’t want to answer.

“She’s a psycho,” Jen comments, and she is even more disturbed when Rio excitedly nods.

“And nothing’s happening, maybe this curse isn’t so bad,” Nicky suggests, though he assumes they won’t be so lucky, and Agatha gives him a look which he is sure means ‘don’t be so stupid,’.

“Does anyone feel…” Alice starts to say.

“What?” Lilia asks.

“I feel lighter,” Alice says amazed, not sure how that is possible, and moments after she says that everyone hears the sound of sizzling as Lilia gasps and yells.

“What is it, Lilia? What’s wrong?” Nicky asks worried.

“It burns!” Lilia exclaims, as she falls to her knees.

“What’s doing that to her? how do we stop it?” Jen asks, becoming upset, having no idea what is going on. “Alice, protect her!” Jen exclaims.

“Can I borrow this?” Alice asks, taking Rio’s knife from here which she uses to draw a circle around Lilia as she chants in Latin.

“Get it off me! It burns it burns!” Lilia yells, but as soon as Alice finishes the spell it is clear that Lilia is no longer in pain.

“I need you to draw one of those circles around me, right now,” Jen comments, as she really doesn’t want to go through what Lilia just went through.

“Are you okay?” Alice asks Lilia concerned.

“So, breaking a curse,” Nicky says, trying to get everyone to focus on what they need to do. “Smudge sticks? A salt bath?” Nicky asks, reciting everything he remembers reading. “What if we locate and reason with the witch who cast the curse?” Nicky asks, looking at his mama to see what she thinks about that, noticing that his mom is just sitting on the couch reading a newspaper, completely unphased, as he does.

“Once vengeance is loose, you can’t real it back in,” Agatha says, knowing that.

“So, what do we do?” Nicky asks his Mama.

“The only way to end a curse is to face it,” Lilia reveals, and once she does Jen yells in pain.

As soon as she hears Jen yell Alice once again uses Rio’s knife to carve a circle around Jen as she cats the protection spell, and as she does Nicky realises something.

“Her shoulders,” Nicky says, as he notices burns on Jen’s shoulders, burns in an exact pattern that Alice finds familiar.

“Do I have one too?” Lilia says, moving her top down to reveal that she has the same marks as Jen, and as she does everyone hears a rumbling in the distance.

“Do you hear that?” Nicky asks worried, and everyone is horrified by the sound they hear.

“What is that?” Jen asks confused.

“That’s the curse,” Rio reveals, still seemingly unphased by everything.

“The backwards record,” Nicky realises.

“What’s the song forward?” Lilia asks, and as she does Alice checks, and is horrified by what she sees as she realises it’s her mother’s song.

“I’ll do my best,” Nicky says, looking around and not seeing the people he wants to see most. “Where are Agatha and Rio?” Nicky asks, feeling concerned about them.

“Agatha said she needed to stretch her legs, Rio followed,” Alice explains.

“How long have they been gone?” Nicky asks worried. “Should we go looking?” Nicky asks, feeling concerned about his mothers.

“Definitely not,” Lilia comments, not needed her powers to know it would be a very bad idea for them to follow Agatha and Rio right now. “It seemed like something they needed to talk about alone,” Lilia explains.

“Oh,” Nicky mutters, not sure how to feel about that, as the implication in Lilia’s words are clear.

“They have some kind of history, right?” Alice asks. “I wasn’t imagining the tension?” Alice asks.

“Oh, they definitely do,” Jen confirms. “Which is exactly why I have no intention to follow them and figure out what they are doing,” Jen comments, having a suspicion that she knows exactly what they are doing, but not wanting it to be confirmed, and Nicky pulls a face which no one else notices as he realises what Jen is implying, as while he does want his mother’s back together he doesn’t want to actually think about them being together.

“I second that,” Alice comments, as like Jen she suspects she knows what Agatha and Rio are doing, but she really doesn’t want her suspicion to be confirmed. “So how about we all try to get some rest,” Alice suggests. “You definitely could use it,” Alice says to Nicky, being sure that even with Jen’s healing he isn’t completely one hundred percent.

“Yeah, I could,” Nicky confirms. “But is it safe to rest here?” Nicky asks concerned, knowing he would feel better if he knew where his moms were.

“Probably not,” Lilia admits. “But we should try to anyway, just stay together,” Lilia says, and Nicky frowns as he can’t help but think about how his mothers aren’t with them.

At Lilia’s words it is clear that both Jen and Alice were tried but just waiting to be told that it’s okay to rest, and once they get that reassurance, they both lay down, and make themselves comfortable, Jen making a sleep mask for herself as she does.

As the others lie down Nicky debates going in search for his mothers, but considering everything the others have implied he knows that wouldn’t be a good idea, and so instead of going in search of his mothers Nicky lays on the ground, and using Agatha’s jacket as a pillow, falls asleep without too much trouble.

AN2: So, I don’t usually write smut, because I don’t think I do a good job of it, so I apologize if it wasn’t very good.

Chapter 24

Chapter 24

AN: Thank you so much for the support to the last chapter. It means everything to me. So, this is a bit of a supersized chapter as I couldn’t figure out where the place to split it. Hope you like. Please let me know what you think. I’ll post the next chapter in around 12 hours, maybe a little longer.

Between the fact that time moves differently on the Road, and the fact that Rio experiences time differently, Rio has no idea how long she has been holding Agatha as she sleeps, but she does know it gives her a feeling of peace, of belonging, that she doesn’t remember feeling for a long time.

As she knows Agatha so well, because she has spent so many years, watching her sleep Rio realises the second Agatha starts to wake up, and when she sees Agatha’s beautiful blue eyes looking at her Rio smiles at her.

“How’d you sleep?” Rio asks.

“Better than I have in a long time,” Agatha admits, even though she knows that technically she cannot remember the last three years.

“Good,” Rio says, as that’s what she wants for Agatha, and she leans down and gives Agatha a gentle kiss, and after a few moments they break apart. As soon as they break apart Rio notices the look on Agatha’s face. “Are you alright?” Rio asks concerned, as she knows the look on Agatha’s face well enough to know that something is bothering her.

“I think the next trial is going to be mine,” Agatha admits, as the purple hue and the purple flowers that are now around The Road, seems to indicate that.

“If it is we’ll deal with it,” Rio assures Agatha.

“Just like before?” Agatha asks, as she feels Rio rub her hand up and down her hip, thinking about the last time they were on the road.

“Just like before,” Rio assures her, as she feels Agatha lean back into her a little more.

“We should probably go back and join the others,” Agatha realises, even though she would like to remain in Rio’s arms.

“Yeah, we probably should,” Rio admits, but before doing that she leans down and gives Agatha one more kiss before they both break apart and get ready to re-join the others.

Having no idea what his mothers are doing, but feeling a very concerned about them, Nicky is wide awake in the clearing while Jen, Alice, and Lilia are all asleep. Not being able to keep in his concern any longer Nicky stands up, leaving Agatha’s jacket on the ground, and is just about to go searching for his moms when Rio, who is now fully dressed, walks into the clearing.

“Rio? Is everything okay? Where’s Agatha?” Nicky asks, knowing that his voice is portraying just how concerned he is feeling.

“She’s fine,” Rio assures Nicky, immediately becoming suspicious of his concern. “She’ll join us soon,” Rio explains, giving Nicky a pondering look.

“Good,” Nicky says, sounding relieved about that.

“You really care, don’t you?” Rio asks, and Nicky immediately realises that he is in trouble because Rio has a look on his face which he knows means she is trying to make sense of something.

“I do,” Nicky says, honestly a little surprised that the Sigil didn’t activate, and Rio takes a step towards him, making Nicky realises, that in all there planning, they made a mistake in not considering that Rio would be suspicious of the fact that such powerful magic was being used to hide him.

“Do you know who you really are?” Rio asks, and Nicky feels the Sigil working, preventing him from answering, but before he can think of a solution that will allow him to give some form of an answer, they are both distracted by Lilia gasping, and bolting upright, causing everyone else to wake up.

“They’re coming, we have to go,” Lilia says panicked.

“What?” Alice asks confused, as everyone in the clearing look at Lilia for answers about what is going on.

“The summoning spell, we left the door open,” Lilia reveals, and because he knows who is after him, and his mama, Nicky has a suspicion that he knows how bad that is.

“What are you talking about? What did you see?” Alice asks confused.

“Go on, Lilia, tell them,” Rio says, as now that the Salem Seven have joined them on the Road, she can feel them, sense their souls, being able to do so because there are so few people on the Road. While she can tell that they are on The Road what she can’t tell is exactly where they are.

“The Salem Seven,” Lilia says and Jen gasp.

“Black robes, working in creepy perfect unison?” Nicky asks, even though he already knows, because he knows that everyone else has to understand just how bad what they are facing is, and Lilia nods.

“When Agatha killed her original coven…” Lilia starts to explain.

“By stealing their power,” Jen adds, once again making Nicky feel annoyed, but before he can say something about that his mom beats him to it.

“Because her own mother tried to have her executed,” Rio says, an edge to her voice, as she will not let anyone talk badly about Agatha when it comes to this particular matter, especially because they don’t know the real story.

“Executed?” Nicky mutters shocked as while he knew bits and pieces of what happened between his mother and Evanora, as he felt the magic that was used when he went to Salem, he didn’t know the specific details as it was something his mom tried to protect him from.

“Are you really defending a noted serial killer, you creepy lurker?” Jen asks, having not heard what Nicky muttered, and Rio becomes angrier at Jen, feelings Nicky shares.

“Come on, someone finish the story,” Alice requests, as she has never even heard about what happened.

“When Agatha murdered her sisters witches, she spared their young children,” Lilia explains, and both Alice and Jen are surprised by that, while the others already knew.

“Yeah, and then they became a feral, hive-minded cover bent on revenge,” Rio reveals, as Agatha who is now dressed, comes running back into the clearing.

“Whoa, ah, the moral of the stories kids, is finish what you started,” Agatha says as she picks up her jacket from where Nicky dropped it. “Also, mercy is overrated,” Agatha says as she puts her jacket back on. “All right everyone, pack up your shit! Let’s go!” Agatha exclaims, and as soon as she does everyone goes running.

As soon as Agatha tells them to go everyone starts to run, only Agatha, Nicky, and Rio realising just how much danger they are in, though Lilia has a suspicion. After about a minute of running the group gets to what seems like an enclosed path which is covered either side in branches in the walls of the path.

“Oh jeez! That was ahead of us,” Jen says as they hear a wolf bark, most of the group knowing that the Salem Seven are able to turn into Animals, and then seconds later they hear the members of the Salem seven scream, and they also hear Lilia scream too.

“That’s behind us,” Alice realises.

“They’re surrounding us,” Nicky reveals, as he can ‘feel’ their magic, feel how intensely their magic is corrected, which means he can tell where each of them are.

“We’re trapped,” Lilia says panicked and as he does Nicky gets an idea.

“Sorry Mama,” Nicky thinks to himself, feeling guilty about what he is about to suggest because he knows it will lack the significance it should have, but he honestly has no other ideas. “What about a hexenbesen?” Nicky asks, avoiding looking at both his moms as he suggests it because he knows that their first hexenbesen together was meant to be special, it wasn’t meant to be a means to survive.

“Brooms? Horrible idea,” Lilia says.

“Absolutely not,” Jen says.

“Yeah!” Rio says.

“That’s a terrible idea,” Agatha

“Yes,” Rio once more says, and it amuses Nicky to know the person who has spent the last eight years telling him he is not allowed to fly is now the one who is agreeing to the idea.

“Well, if you’re all too cool for a practical means of escape…” Nicky says, feeling the Seven get closer, but before he can even give another argument, they all hear the Salem Seven screech which causes them all to gasp.

“No, booms are great,” Alice says approvingly, and Agatha, Rio, Alice, Jen and Lilia all start to pull branches off the walls of the path so that they can use them to create brooms.

“No, no, no,” Jen says annoyed as she pulls off her broom.

“This is so humiliating,” Lilia says, as she starts to put her broom together.

“Why does your generation hate them so much?” Nicky asks Lilia curious, as he knows about his mama’s feelings about brooms thanks to his mom, but what he doesn’t know is why Lilia is so against them, and he is curious about that.

“Brooms have been co-opted by the holiday industrial complex as an absurd emblem of our culture,” Lilia explains. “Worse yet, they’re an obvious symbol of female domesticity,” Lilia explains, as she, like Rio, Agatha, Jen and Alice continue to put their brooms together.

“And they’re basics,” Jen says and as he does Nicky hears his moms chanting in Latin and so he turns to look at them, and he sees them walking around each other, performing the ritual for a hexenbesen, and once they are done they exchange their brooms, Nicky noticing their hands lingering on one another just a little longer than he would expect, as Jen and Lilia both start their ritual too.

“It’s about selfishness Teen,” Agatha tells Nicky, wanting to give him this particular lesson.

“Oh, is it?” Jen asks annoyed, being pretty sure that it is pretty hypocritical for Agatha to be the one saying that. “Tell us more,” Jen says.

“We fly together, or not at all,” Agatha reveals, ignoring Jen.

“Hey,” Alice says, tapping Nicky on his shoulder with a broom and he turns to look at her.

“I get one?” Nicky asks, as he wasn’t sure how that was going to work, wasn’t sure if he was going to have to ride on the back of one of his mothers’ brooms.

“If you give me one back yeah,” Alice confirms, and as soon as he hears that Nicky hurries to the wall, needing to climb a little and pulls a branch free. As soon as he pulls the branch free Nicky passes it to his mama, but before he can climb down, he hears an owl hoot, feels magic he knows belong to a member of the Salem Seven, and he is thrown onto his back, as he is attacked by a member of the Salem Seven.

Not even thinking about it Nicky is about to use his magic to fight back when he hears his mom’s voice say, ‘be careful using your magic, it makes your identity clear,’ but before he can even think if it will be worth it Alice uses the broom she is holding to hit the Salem seven member.

“Get of him!” Alice yells, as Nicky gets back onto his feet.

“Teen, hurry! Just finish the ritual!” Agatha exclaims, feeling afraid that something is going to happen to him. “Finish the ritual!” Agatha exclaims, knowing that they need to get moving, and Nicky and Alice do exactly that. “All right, let’s go,” Agatha says, the second Alice and Nicky finish their ritual.

As soon as Agatha says go she, Rio, Alice, Jen, and Lilia jump onto their brooms and start to fly without a problem while Nicky runs behind them, feeling confused, as he has no idea what to do because his mom wanted his mama to teach him everything about a Hexenbesen.

“Wait? How do we do this?” Nicky asks confused.

“Keep up, Teen,” Agatha tells him.

“Okay, you’ve got this, you’ve got this,” Nicky says to himself, and he finally manages to jump onto the broom, and fly for the first time in his life.

“Try praying to the divine mother, Kiddo,” Lilia tells Nicky, who can’t help but look at his mama, as he knows this was supposed to be something they shared when they both knew who they were, when they both understood the significance.

“We’ve got to get off the road,” Alice tells the others.

“Move!” Agatha says, and in perfect unison they fly up into the sky, flying together as a real coven.

“This is incredible,” Alice says amazed

“I haven’t done this in centuries,” Lilia admits, feeling amazed, at peace, as they continue to fly.

As they fly as his mama watches his mom Nicky can’t help but think about how this is something he has wanted to do for so long. While it’s not perfect, and is definitely something he wants to repeat when his mama knows who he is, it still feels pretty incredible to fly with both his moms and other people who are becoming important to them all, even if his mothers would never admit that fact.

“Why haven’t we been doing this all along?” Nicky asks amazed, but as soon as he asks the question it is answered as they are all flipped upside down.

“What is going on?” Lilia asks confused.

“The road is forcing us down,” Agatha explains, as they are forced to the ground, and while Rio cackles in amusement everyone else screams in terror.

“We’re going to crash!” Alice exclaims terrified.

“It won’t leave us,” Jen says, and as they get closer to the ground the brooms even out and they are able to keep flying, only a little above the ground.

“Okay, we’re okay,” Jen assures the others, and as she does Nicky sees something in the distance.

“THERE! The next trial,” Nicky says, pointing to a cabin, and the group fly there, needing to fly through a member of the Salem seven to get inside, but managing to all barrel inside before something else bad happens.

As soon as the group get into the cabin Rio realises that Agatha’s suspicion was right, and this is her trial. Just like the last trial everyone has been transformed into different clothes, in this case 80s sleepover wear, while the ‘house’ itself looks like a sleepover treehouse.

“Okay. All right. Okay, okay, we’re okay,” Agatha, who was the last one into the trial, says, trying to reassure everyone else.

“No, we’re not!” Jen exclaims horrified. “The entire Halloween aisles outside waiting for us!” Jen exclaims.

“And it doesn’t look like they can get in, does it, Jen?” Agatha asks, and Nicky realises she is right as he can’t ‘feel’ their magic. “So, all we have to do is complete the trial and continue on before they can reach us. Okay,” Agatha says to the others, with the exception of Nicky, who is looking for something, are looking around.

“How? Kiss, marry, kill?” Alice asks, as that’s what it seems like from the outfits they are wearing.

“Flying on a broom,” Nicky admits.

“Whose trial is this?” Nicky asks.

“Agatha’s,” Rio answers, without hesitation, knowing that she would have been able to tell that even if she and Agatha didn’t talk about it earlier.

“How’d you know?” Nicky asks his mom, curious about how she realised so quickly, but also having a really bad feeling about how this is going to go, but to his relief he feels nothing that tells him someone is a certainty to die, but he also knows he can’t be sure of that without touching everyone.

“A blood moon. When the veil between the living and the dead is at it’s thinnest,” Lilia explains, pointing to a picture, Nicky being the only one in the room who currently knows that there was a time when the veil was even thinner.

“Wait, I thought talking to the dead was your department,” Nicky says to Lilia, as while he knows a little about his mama’s abilities, he doesn’t know everything as Rio always knew that Agatha would want to teach him herself.

“Oh, common misconception, I read people, I read time, but talking to spirits was just a con,” Lilia reveals.

“And who better to commune with the dead than someone who’s put so many in a grave?” Rio asks, using her knife which has been transformed into a brush a microphone which she points at Agatha as a Ouija board flies out and onto a table, which Nicky walks over to.

“We have to Ouija,” Nicky says, having a bad feeling about this, and this time he is sure it has nothing to do with his ability to sense death, and as soon as he says that the timers on the watches everyone is wearing start to beep.

“It’s not a verb,” Agatha says, really not liking the idea of this, but as she glances at Rio she gives her an encouraging loo, Rio’s subtle way of assuring her that everything will be okay.

Ah, English,” Nicky says as while he could easily read the Spanish, he doesn’t want to deal with the questions that will come along with that. “Number one do not use the Ouija board alone,” Nicky reads, and everyone gestures as if to say they aren’t alone. “Number two. Do not speak over each other,” Nicky says, and as soon as he says that everyone starts to speak over each other. “THREE!” Nicky exclaims, trying to get everyone’s attention so that they stop talking over each other. “Do not taunt the spirits,” Nicky reads, and once he does everyone turns to Agatha.

“What?” Agatha asks.

“I repeat, do not taunt the spirits,” Nicky reads, looking at his Mama. “Four, do not ask about death,” Nicky says, fighting to keep the amusement out of his voice at that, but only Agatha and Rio notice, causing them to exchange looks as that is another piece of evidence that supports their theory. “Five, always end your session with goodbye,” Nicky reads. “Six, do not, under any circumstances, remove your hand from the planchette, if you do a spirit will be released,” Nicky reads.

“What does it say on the back?” Lilia asks.

“For ages three and up,” Nicky says once he reads the back.

“Okay,” Lilia says and and everyone except for Agatha sit down around the small coffee table.

“Wonder who’s waiting for you,” Nicky says to his mama, dreading what is going to happen.

“And with what trauma,” Jen says, in a tone of voice that suggests she is going to enjoy Agatha’s suffering.

Once she is sitting down Agatha can’t help but think about how much she doesn’t want do this, and everyone puts their hands on the planchette, Nicky using the opportunity to briefly graze everyone else’s fingers and confirm for his own reassurance that no one is a certainty to die soon.

“Mother, Maiden, Crone, spirits be known,” Agatha says purposely saying the goddesses in the wrong order, and because of that she makes the planchette moves, while making it seem like she isn’t doing exactly that. “I can hear something, shh,” Agatha says.

“Yes,” Jen reads.

Well, let’s get to it, right,” Agatha says, and everyone puts their fingers back on the planchette. “Maiden, mother, crone, spirts be known,” Agatha says, purposely saying it right, and as soon as she does the lights flicker, and everyone feels the wind rustling. “Who is here with us tonight?” Agatha asks, and as soon as she does the planchette starts to move again, this time on it’s own.

“Stop it! Let her go! Alice exclaims. “What are you doing? You’re hurting her,” Alice says, and once she does Lilia turns on the lights, causing Agatha to disappear. “Jen, Jen,” Alice says, hurrying over to Jen to make sure she is okay, as everyone comes to the middle of the room.

“My coven risked everything to kill her, and you fools have willingly joined her,” Evanora says, and while Nicky isn’t overly surprised by that because of the pieces he has put together that doesn’t make it any easier to hear, as Rio puts her knife back.

“So, what do we do? Do we banish her?” Jen asks, looking at Lilia for help as she assumes Lilia will know.

“Emotions ties them to this plane,” Lilia explains. “They have unfinished business,” Lilia explains.

“So, let’s finish her business,” Nicky says, knowing that he has to do whatever he has to do to make sure Evanora doesn’t hurt his mama again.

“Okay,” Jen says.

“What do you want?” Nicky asks Evanora and because of her suspicions about who Nicky is Agatha knows she doesn’t want him anywhere near Evanora.

“You must finish the Witches Road, without Agatha,” Evanora says, and neither Nicky nor Rio have any intention of allowing that to happen.

“She means punish Agatha,” Lilia realises.

“Leave her with me,” Evanora says.

“No,” Nicky and Rio yell together.

“No way,” Rio adds.

“A minute ago, you were ready to slit her throat,” Jen says surprised, not understanding Rio at all.

“Yeah, well, her mother can’t have her,” Rio exclaims, knowing there is no way she is going to let that happen, and as she does Evanora moves towards Rio as Agatha climbs down the stairs from the upper level.

“Mom? Why do you hate me still?” Agatha asks, as that is what she has always wanted to know.

“You were born evil,” Evanora says, and Rio knows that is not true. “I ought to have killed you the moment you left my body,” Evanora says and once she does both Rio and Nicky, who understands a little more why his mom never talked about Evanora, are devastated to hear that, while Alice, who from her perspective had the most incredible mom, who did everything she could to keep her safe, is horrified.

“We have to go,” Jen says, refusing to let Evanora’s words get to her.

“Jen!” Nicky exclaims, not being able to believe she is suggesting that.

“No, no! There’s no flood here. There’s no fire, the only danger to us in this trial is Agatha Harkness,” Jen says, and as soon as she does Agatha starts to become upset.

“Please, take me with you! Don’t leave me! Please don’t go!” Agatha exclaims, starting to fall apart in a way only Rio has seen before.

“We can’t leave her here!” Nicky says as he tries to reach for Agatha.

“No, no, take me with you! Please, don’t leave me here with her. I can be good, please!” Agatha exclaims, reaching for Nicky, but before she can get close, Evanora flies back into her body, possessing her once again.

“No, not again!” Lilia exclaims.

“Leave her alone!” Alice exclaims, and she sends a blast towards Agatha, hitting her with it.

As he sees Alice’s power hit Agatha, and knowing what is about to happen, Nicky, who realises he feels nothing that says a death is a certainty, knows there is hope and because of that he knows exactly what he needs to do. Running from where he is with Lila and Jen, behind Alice, Nicky recites the phrase that will destroy the Sigil.

“What language is that’s?” Jen asks confused, hearing what Nicky is saying, as Evanora is ejected from Agatha, who starts to siphon Alice’s power, her life-force, as Nicky, feeling as the Sigil is destroyed, gets to where he wants to be, directly to Agatha’s left.

“Mama stop!” Nicky exclaims, everyone being able to hear what he is saying because the Sigil is destroyed. “It’s me, Nicky!” Nicky says, raising his arm, in the same way Alice has raised hers, not sure what he is going to do, but knowing he has to do something.

“NICKY NO!” Rio, who has just been bombarded with her memories, yells, her voice full of absolute horror.

Chapter 25

Chapter 25

AN: Thank you so much for the incredible response to the last chapter. I do feel a little bad about the cliffhanger.

So, the next chapter won’t be out until after the final comes out, in fact, it will be posted closer to my normal time of 6pm my time. Also, I have written the last chapter of this story, unless I change something it will be 37 chapters in total. Again, thank you so much for your support, you have no idea what it means to me.

As she hears her son confirm who he is, and hears the absolute horror in her love’s voice, Agatha is able to do something she has never done before, turn away from someone she is siphoning power from and look at her son, causing Alice to be a little weakened, but still alive.

“Nicky?” Agatha asks, looking at him in amazement, tears coming to her eyes, as for over a century this is all she has wanted, her son back.

“Mama,” Nicky says, lowering his arms, letting go of the magic that was on the tips of his fingers about to be released, before hurrying towards her and doing what he has been wanting to do for the last eight years; hugging her; “I’ve missed you so much,” Nicky says as he hugs his mama tightly, and as she watches them hug Rio smiles, feeling her heart full of love, knowing what this would mean to both of them.

“I’ve missed you too, so much,” Agatha says, pulling back a little so she can look at her son, memorize everything about the way he looks now. “I love you,” Agatha assures her son.

“I love you too, Mama,” Nicky responds, feeling beyond amazed, as this is what he has wanted for so long.

“How? How are you here?” Agatha asks, feeling both amazed and confused about how this is possible, as the Sigil breaking hasn’t helped her with that.

“Mom,” Nicky answers, and as he does Agatha looks over at Rio, but doesn’t move away from Nicky, while Jen and Lilia are checking on Alice, wanting to make sure she is okay.

“When Thanos used the power of all the Infinity Stones in one go, he didn’t only cause half of the universe to disappear, but caused the entire universe to fall into chaos,” Rio explains. “The veil was made thinner than it has ever been before. I was able to punch through it, I found Nicky and brought him back with me,” Rio explains, feeling that is the best explanation to give at the moment.

“You always said that was impossible,” Agatha says to Rio, remembering the fights they had about that, trying to comprehend exactly what that means.

“It was, until it wasn’t,” Rio explains.

“Mom was weak for days after she brought me back,” Nicky tells his mama. “She actually slept,” Nicky tells his mama, wanting to help her understand what that means, as while he did not understand the significance of that as the time he does now, and right away she does, and Agatha knows that is something she is going to talk to Rio about at a later point, when it is just the two of them.

“Wait, Thanos. That was eight years ago,” Agatha realizes, as she starts to comprehend just how much she has missed. “Why didn’t you…” Agatha starts to ask, looking at Rio, anger in her voice.

“The Darkhold,” Rio says, before Agatha can even finish the question, the accusation, as she knows exactly what Agatha is going to say, as she was expecting it.

“You couldn’t find me,” Agatha realizes, anger slipping away, knowing that it would be easier if she could blame someone for the fact she missed out on eight years with her son, but the truth is she is the only one to blame.

“We tried, Mama, we really did. We never stopped trying to find you,” Nicky assures her, not wanting his mama to think they forget about her.

“As soon as you lost that damn book we travelled to Westview, but….” Rio starts to explain.

“It was too late, and I was under Wanda’s spell,” Agatha realizes. “You been in Westview the last three years?” Agatha asks, looking between Nicky and Rio, feeling that she has a lot of questions about that.

“Trying to figure out how to break the spell, yeah,” Nicky tells his mama. “Mama, I’m so sorry I couldn’t break it sooner, I’ve tried, I’ve really tried,” Nicky assures his mama, needing to make that clear, guilt perfectly clear in his voice.

“Oh Sweetheart, you have nothing to apologize for, absolutely nothing,” Agatha says, before hugging him once again, knowing that the knowledge that she has lost eight years with her son, and Rio, because of her own selfish choices, her own quest for power, and that Nicky blames herself, is the biggest punishment she could ever receive.

“The door!” Alice, who has been helped to her feet, says as the way out of the trial appears.

“I don’t understand, how is that a punishment?” Jen, who now understands why Nicky acted the way he did towards her during the first trial, says.

“Agatha was punished,” Lilia explains. “She learnt what she lost because of her choices, and the effects those choses had on the person she loves most,” Lilia says, understanding exactly what happened. “Agatha, we should go, we don’t know what happens if we stay in a trial after it’s finished,” Lilia advises, trying to do so in the gentlest way.

“She’s right,” Rio says to Agatha, and as an understanding passes between them and Agatha nods.

As the group make their way out of the trial, Jen and Lilia helping Alice, while Agatha keeps her arm around Nicky, they are so distracted that they don’t see a white wisp of energy follow them as they forgot a key rule of using the Ouija board.

As they once again leave a trial the group find themselves back on The Road where there is a green hue to the entire road.

“We should rest,” Lilia suggests, once they have all left the trial, knowing that Alice definitely needs to rest because of how physically she is drained while Agatha, Nicky and Rio could use a rest because of how emotionally drained they clearly are.

“Can we risk that with the Seven?” Jen asks, feeling like they can’t, but she cannot help but look worriedly at Alice, who is alive, but clearly weakened.

“They’re not close,” Nicky reveals, deciding that now everyone knows who he is there is no point in hiding, at least some, of what he can do.

“How do you know?” Agatha asks her son, not knowing why he is clearly so certain about that, and with a sad ache she adds it to the list of things she doesn’t know about her son.

“I can, for lack of a better description, feel magic,” Nicky explains, feeling glad to finally be able to explain that particular ability of his to his mama as he knows he got it because of her. “The Seven are so intertwined, so connected, that their magic feels completely unique. I can tell when they get close; there not close at the moment,” Nicky explains, looking at his mother as he gives the explanation, as she’s the one he wants to talk to, but everyone hears.

“Handy,” Jen comments, feeling that that must be a very unique ability.

“Not always,” Nicky responds, remembering what it felt like to feel the spell his mama was in, and while Agatha is confused by what that means she notices the look on Rio’s face which tells here that there is a story there, one she suspects Nicky won’t want to talk about in front of everyone.

“If we’re going to take some time to rest, we should set up camp,” Lilia tells the others, not addressing what Nicky just said as she understands what it can be like to have an ability that causes sensations so intense that they can be a struggle to deal with.

“I like the sound of that,” Alice admits, feeling pretty exhausted, and considering everything that just happened Agatha knows what she should do.

“Alice, I…” Agatha starts to say, honestly having no idea if she is going to apologize, or explain, but knowing she has to say something, even if she has no idea what.

“It’s okay,” Alice says, surprising Agatha, giving her a reassuring look.

“It’s, okay?” Jen asks, shocked. “She tried to kill you! How can you say that’s okay?”  Jen asks not being able to believe that.

“Because I was paying attention and realize that Agatha wasn’t in control,” Alice says, knowing that, as she felt that when Agatha started to siphon her magic. “So yeah, I’m saying it’s okay,” Alice reveals, making it clear she isn’t going to change her mind about this. “And I’m also saying thank you… Nicky,” Alice says, looking at him, knowing that because of him that she is still alive.

“You’re welcome,” Nicky responds. “I’m just glad I was able to help someone on this damn road,” Nicky says, thinking about Sharon, and causing Agatha and Rio to exchange looks, it being perfectly clear that neither of them understand what that means, but are both extremely concerned about their son’s reaction. “Lilia’s right, we should get a camp set up,” Nicky says, wanting attention off him, and actually working pretty well together for once, the group gets started on setting up a campsite together.

About ten minutes after Nicky suggested getting a fire set up he, Rio, Alice, Jen, and Lilia are sitting around the fire, talking a little, Rio sitting right next to her son, while Agatha is sitting alone. As she sees that Agatha has decided to sit alone rather than joining the group, Rio, who knows that while Agatha might make it seem like she wants to be alone actually wouldn’t want to be, knows what she has to do.

“I’ll be back,” Rio says to her son in a quiet voice, only loud enough for him to hear. “And don’t for a second think we’re not going to talk about the fact that you hid you were hurt,” Rio tells her son, now knowing that he realized he was hurt long before he collapsed.

“I honestly hoping you didn’t remember that,” Nicky admits, though he isn’t overly surprised he didn’t get that lucky.

“Not a chance, Mi Conejtio,” Rio say. “We’re also going to talk about what you almost did,” Rio tells Nicky, his voice only loud enough for him to hear, before walking over to Agatha.

“Mi Conejtio?” Jen asks. “Just how many languages do you speak?” Jen asks, still feeling confused about what language he spoke in to break the Sigil as it was clearly a language no one, other than Rio, and maybe Agatha, have ever heard before.

“A lot,” Nicky answers as he watches his mom sit down next to his mama.

“Are you okay?” Rio asks Agatha a few moments after she sits down next to her, when she realizes that Agatha isn’t going to acknowledge her presence.

“What do you think?” Agatha asks her, feeling that Rio should know better than asking that question.

“I think you’re probably feeling a whole lot right now that you don’t want to admit to, that you have a lot of questions,” Rio assumes, and Agatha silently curses Rio for knowing her so well. “If you want to ask them, I won’t lie,” Rio assures Agatha.

“You never do,” Agatha responds, knowing that, and while there are a lot of things, she wants to know she knows exactly what she wants to know first. “Where there any side effects of bringing him back?” Agatha asks.

“On him or me?” Rio asks, as there are multiple ways she could answer that particular question.

“Both,” Agatha answers.

“He was fine,” Rio assures Agatha. “Took some time to adjust to being back especially considering the changes in the world, but he was fine,” Rio assures Agatha, who visibly relax at that. “I was weakened for a while,” Rio explains, knowing there is no point in lying about that as Nicky already spilled the beans about that.

“Nicky said you slept,” Agatha says, knowing exactly how unusual that is.

“For a couple of days,” Rio admits, and Agatha is beyond shocked about that. “Turns out forcing your way through the veil, even for me, takes a lot of power, takes a lot out of you,” Rio explains, knowing it was worth it.

“But you still did it, you brought him back to us,” Agatha says, still amazed by that.

“As soon as I felt the universe become chaos, I knew I had to try, no matter what it took,” Rio admits.

“Thank you,” Agatha says amazed.

“You don’t have to thank me, Amour, I’m just sorry I couldn’t bring him back to you sooner,” Rio admits.

“Us,” Agatha corrects, reaching out and taking Rio’s hand. “He seems good, happy, you’ve done an amazing job,” Agatha says, as while she feels deep sorrow that she hasn’t been able to be with her son and Rio she is feeling some relief that he seems to be so okay.

“I’ve tried,” Rio admits. “But not a day went by where I didn’t wish you, the real you, were with us,” Rio assures Agatha, who realizes exactly what that means.

“You spent time with Agnes?” Agatha asks, realizing that she doesn’t know what that would have been liked as she only remembers the few days before the spell was broken, not before that.

“We live down the road,” Rio reveals, and while she realizes that makes sense Agatha is more surprised than she would admit as she knows Rio doesn’t tend to stay in the same place long, let alone three years. “Your reality reset every few days. So, we didn’t always know what to expect, but we did what we could to look after you, spend time with you,” Rio explains to Agatha, trying to explain in the most delicate way possible as she knows it’s an incredibly complicated situation and she doesn’t want Agatha to feel guilty about that.

“Did I ever know you? Either of you?” Agatha asks, knowing it was sometimes painful to be around Nicky and just suspect who he was under the Sigil and because of that she can’t imagine what it was like for him to spend time with her if she never knew who he was when he did, while Rio debates the best way to answer as she doesn’t want to cause Agatha pain. “Rio?” Agatha asks, gently prodding when she realizes Rio isn’t answering.

“After we made a failed attempt to break the spell, you always knew I was someone from your past, more often than not someone you hated and was feeling a lot of anger towards,” Rio admits, not wanting to cause Agatha pain, but knowing she said she would be honest. “You never knew who Nicky was, but you did subconsciously look after him, and no matter what couldn’t handle hearing his name,” Rio explains.

“I am so sorry,” Agatha tells Rio, having no idea how Rio would have handled experiencing, potentially years, of her hating her when they saw each other regularly, and feeling even more guilt as she realized the pain she must have caused Nicky by having no idea who he was.

“It’s not your fault,” Rio assures her, as she doesn’t want Agatha to blame herself more than she already is. “There’s only one person to blame,” Rio says, both Agatha and Rio knowing exactly who she is talking about.

“Is she actually dead?” Agatha asks, needing to know that, and knowing that Rio is the one person who would know.

“Yes, but I don’t have much hope she’ll stay that way,” Rio admits, and as she does, she feels Agatha’s hand shiver in hers. “She’ll never hurt you again, never violate you again, I’m not gonna let that happen,” Rio says protectively, and Agatha smiles slightly, it being a long time since she has experienced Rio’s protectiveness, and realizing that it is something she has truly missed. “I’ll go toe to toe with her if I have to,” Rio assures Agatha, who knows that would be quiet the showdown.

“Just like you stood up to mother?” Agatha asks, that having meant everything to her, and Rio nods.

“Agatha, what she said wasn’t true, you were not born evil,” Rio assures Agatha, saying what she has told Agatha before, but also knowing that it will be difficult for Agatha to believe her as she always has.

“Did Nicky know about her before now?” Agatha asks, not addressing what Rio just said as that’s not something she can believe, no matter how many times Rio tries to convince her otherwise, and knowing that while she never told Nicky about his grandmother, she doesn’t know what Rio has told him over the last eight years.

“He knew a little, not a lot,” Rio admits. “We went to Salem when we were looking for you,” Rio explains.

“Salem? Why? You know I’d never go back there,” Agatha says, a little surprised that Rio would choose to go back there.

“I know, but I wanted to show Nicky where he came from, where we met,” Rio admits. “We went to the Clearing,” Rio reveals, and as she does Agatha has a sinking suspicion about something, she just hopes she is wrong.

“Please don’t tell me he could feel the magic used there, even after all this time,” Agatha says, knowing that if Rio and Nicky went to Salem while searching for her then that would have happened before he was thirteen, and if he could feel what happened then that would have been a lot for a kid to handle.

“He could, but that’s not all he could feel,” Rio reveals, and Agatha gives her an interested look, actually dreading what Rio is going to explain next. “Agatha, Nicky did inherit abilities from me,” Rio reveals.

“What kind of abilities?” Agatha asks, glancing over to where Nicky is happily talking with Alice.
