Right now, you’re still trapped, buried beneath the Scarlett Witches’ spell, but if you are watching this it means that I finally figured out how to break it, and if that’s the case I really hope I figure it out soon; Mama I’m really sorry it’s taken so long, I’m really sorry I’ve let you down”

“Oh sweetheart, you haven’t let me down, you never could, you have nothing to feel sorry for,” Agatha says, knowing she will have to tell actual Nicky as soon as he gets home.

“I know Mom is trying to remember everything about me so that she can tell you stories when we break the spell, well there are a few things I want to tell you about Mom. The first is, she loves you, so much, and she’s taken really amazing care of me, she’s trying to be strong, and do everything alone, but I know how much she needs you,”

Watching the videos Agatha has to fight back tears as she continues to watch her son talk, explain so many thigs she wishes she got to experience with him, and Rio. Even though it is painful for her Agatha continues to watch the videos as she wants to know everything that Nicky wanted her to know.

Having no idea that Agatha has been watching videos their son recorded for her Rio, who was gone longer than she wanted to be, is arriving back home. As she walks into the house, she notices Agatha sitting in the same spot she herself has sat in so many times.

“You’re sitting in my spot,” Rio tells Agatha.

“So, I’ve been told,” Agatha says, turning to look at her, and as she does Rio notices the look on her face.

“Agatha, what’s wrong?” Rio asks concerned, as she walks over to Agatha.

“Did you know Nicky’s recorded videos over the last year? Of things he wanted me to know?” Agatha asks.

“He never told me, but I realised,” Rio admits, as she sits down with Agatha. “You watched them?” Rio asks, as that’s what she assumes, and Agatha nods.

“Rio, I am so sorry about causing you so much pain, about not being there when you needed me,” Agatha says, leaning forward.

“Agatha, its okay, I’m okay,” Rio assures her, not wanting Agatha to carry around anymore guilt than she is already carrying. “You’re you again, we’re together, Nicky’s okay, you finally have a supportive coven, that’s all that matters,” Rio tells her wife.

“I never thought I deserved any of those things,” Agatha admits, looking down.

“I know,” Rio admits, reaching out and putting her hand against Agatha’s cheek, gently moving her face so that Agatha is looking at her. “But you do. You’re not who your mother made you believe you are, who you tried to make the world see you as; you Agatha Harkness are incredible, you are good, and you need to start believing that,” Rio tells her, as she feels Agatha lean into her hand.

“I’ll try,” Agatha says, knowing it is going to be very difficult for her, and Rio leans forward and kisses her, a gentle kiss, and after a few moments they break apart.

“Where is Nicky?” Rio asks curious, realising she should have asked that earlier.

“He went the library, but he messaged me saying he was going to meet Eddie and bring him here,” Agatha explains.

“I see,” Rio realises, checking the clock. “Which means we don’t have long,” Rio says. “You figured out how you are going to threaten him yet?” Rio asks curious.

“Not yet, I’ve got a few ideas,” Agatha says, and Rio laughs.

“Oh, this is going to be fun,” Rio confirms, exchanging amused looks with Agatha, one she returns resulting in both of them breaking down in laughter before they start to discuss just what they plan for Nicky’s boyfriend.

A while after he left to go to the library, feeling incredibly nervous, Nicky is walking towards his house with Eddie by his side.

“So, your mom is well enough to come home?” Eddie asks, still trying to make sense of everything.

“Yep,” Nicky says, and he turns to look at Eddie. “Um, so you’re going to recognize her,” Nicky says, knowing that Eddie has seen ‘Agnes’ around town. “But you need to know that who you’re meeting tonight is who she really is, that the person you meet tonight is my mama. Who I’ve been trying really hard to get back,” Nicky explains.

“Okay,” Eddie says, feeling very confused. “I know you have trust issues, so I’m never going to push you, but when you’re ready to give it, I’d really like an explanation,” Eddie admits, as he has long accepted that there are things Nicky doesn’t talk about, but that doesn’t mean he isn’t curious.

“I know, you deserve one,” Nicky admits. “Just not tonight,” Nicky tells Eddie.

“Okay,” Eddie responds.

“Thank you for being so understanding,” Nicky says.

“You don’t have to thank me for that,” Eddie assures him, giving a smile. “We should probably head inside,” Eddie says.

“Yeah, guess we should,” Nicky says, and taking Eddie’s hand he heads into the house. “Mom? Mama?” Nicky asks, as both he and Eddie walk into the house and Nicky sees no sign of his moms.

“Right here,” Rio’s voice says, and Nicky turns to see his moms walking down the stairs. “Hi Eddie,” Rio greats, with an over the top grin that even Nicky finds very creepy as it is very unlike his mom.

“Hi… Mrs Scratch,” Eddie great, clearly nervous, and clearly recognizing Agatha, which is not helping with the confusion he is feeling.

“Eddie, I’d like you to meet my mama, Agatha,” Nicky introduces, slightly stressing ‘Agatha’, feeling suspicious about what his moms are up to. “Mama, this is my boyfriend Eddie,” Nicky introduces.

“Eddie, it’s lovely to finally meet you,” Agatha says, sticking out her hand for Eddie to shake.

“You too, ma’am,” Eddie responds, clearly having no idea how to refer to Agatha as she squeezes his hand a little too tight.

“Please, call me Agatha,” Agatha responds, and as she does there is a knock on the door.

“Didn’t we tell Alice not to knock?” Nicky asks confused.

“We did,” Rio assures him, walking to the door, knowing exactly why Alice knocked.

“Who’s Alice?” Eddie asks Nicky in a quiet voice, clearly confused.

“Nicky’s adoptive sister,” Agatha responds, having heard the question, and Eddie looks incredible confused about that as in all the time together Nicky has never mentioned an Alice, or a sister, as Rio opens the door and reveals not just Alice standing on the step, but Jen and Lilia too.

“You’ve got to be kidding me,” Nicky mutters, as he sees the trio.

“Hey, hope it’s okay a couple more people join us,” Alice says, purposely not revealing that it was Agatha and Rio’s idea.

“Of course not, the more the merrier,” Rio assures her.

“And it works perfectly because we just happened to order extra pizza,” Agatha reveals.

“You don’t say,” Nicky says, looking between his moms and realising that it was their entire plan, to have Eddie interrogated not just by them but by the whole Coven. “Eddie, that’s Alice, and this is Jen, and Lilia my…” Nicky says, trailing off as he realises, he has no idea how to introduce them.

“Aunts,” Lilia supplies. “It’s an absolute pleasure to meet you,” Lilia says.

“Uh, you too,” Eddie says, feeling more confused with every minute.

“How about we move this conversation into the living room, no point talking on the stairs,” Jen suggests.

“Good idea,” Nicky says, and everyone heads into the living room, Alice asking Eddie to tell them a little about himself as they go.

A little while after Nicky realised that it’s not going to be just his mothers interrogating, and scaring, Eddie but everyone he now considers family, the pizza has arrived and because of that Nicky has headed to the kitchen to grab plates and cups.

“Are you alright?” Agatha, who has followed his son, asks as Nicky starts to collect everything they need.

“Yeah,” Nicky assures her. “I just didn’t expect the entire family interrogation,” Nicky admits, and it fills Agatha’s heart to know that her son has entire coven of people who he considers family, that he isn’t alone.

“We couldn’t pass up the opportunity,” Agatha reveals, and Nicky rolls his eyes.

“I get it, would have appreciated some warning, but I get it,” Nicky admits.

“No warning is what makes it fun,” Agatha reveals, and Nicky laughs a that.

“Mama… I may complain but this, you back, teasing me with my boyfriend, disturbing me with Mom, is everything I’ve ever wanted, everything I’ve ever wished for,” Nicky admits. “So even if I complain…. I don’t mean it, because this means… so damn much to me,” Nicky admits.

“It means a lot to me too,” Agatha assures her son, walking over to her son, who she hugs. “Nicky, I watched all your videos, and you need to know, you didn’t let me down, ever,” Agatha assures her son, wanting to make that clear.

“It felt like I did,” Nicky admits.

“You didn’t, you never could,” Agatha assures her son, kissing his head before they break apart. “We should probably get back out there,” Agatha says.

“Yeah, who knows how everyone is traumatising Eddie,” Nicky says, honestly a little worried about that.

“We’re all pulling our punches, promise,” Agatha tells her son.

“Appreciate it,” Nicky says, then he gets an idea. “You thinking what I’m thinking Mama?” Nicky asks with a smirk, as he makes his magick dance around his fingers.

“Definitely,” Agatha responds, and they both use their magicks to move the plates, cups, and drinks into the hands before heading back into the living room to join everyone else.

As Nicky walks back into the living room and re-joins his boyfriend, moms, and new family Nicky realises that he went down The Road to get his mama back and along the way he gained something he didn’t realise he wanted, didn’t know he needed, an entire family. While is moms have always, and always will be, more than enough for him it feels pretty incredible to know that they aren’t the only ones who love him, who will be there for him, no matter what.

Chapter 37

Chapter 37

AN: So, here we are, the last chapter. I just want to say, THANK YOU. The response you have given to this story has been beyond incredible, I could have never imagined it; it means more to me than words can say. I really hope you like this conclusion. Please let me know what you think.

October 31st 2026

Three weeks have passed since Nicky and Rio broke the spell Agatha was under, and little over two weeks have passed since Agatha, Rio, Nicky, Alice, Jen, and Lilia returned from the road and ever since they have been doing their best to get used to the lives they gained; something which has involved all six of them still spending a lot of time together.

It’s a Saturday evening and Nicky, who is dressed in a black tuxedo, is in the kitchen of the home he, his moms, and Alice have been living in together since returning from The Road. Moving around the kitchen Nicky is checking, and double checking, that all the food, that is covering every surface in the kitchen, is perfect when Alice, who is wearing a dark maroon suit, walks into the room.

“You really did go all out,” Alice says, taking notice of everything Nicky has cooked.

“I had to,” Nicky responds. “I had to make today as special as possible,” Nicky explains.

“Nicky, it’s already going to be special, there’s no need for you to put extra pressure on yourself,” Alice says, though she does understand why he has.

“I know… I just wanted to make it extra so,” Nicky admits, as he felt like he owed it to his moms.

“Fair enough,” Alice responds, realising there is nothing she can say to convince Nicky he doesn’t have to try so hard. “So, is Eddie coming?” Alice asks curious, deciding a change of subject is best.

“He might come to the celebration later, but not the actual ceremony,” Nicky admits. “After he passed that whole group interrogation Mom and Mama said I could tell them everything but…” Nicky starts to say, before trailing off, as he avoids looking at Alice.

“You’re not sure you’re ready?” Alice asks in a gentle tone of voice, having learnt over the last few weeks that sometimes Nicky need some gentle probing to talk about what is actually going on with him.

“Exactly,” Nicky says with a nod. “Especially when we still haven’t decided if we’re staying in Westview,” Nicky admits.

“That’s fair enough, but take it from me, not letting yourself experience something that could be good for you because you’re worried about losing it is no way to live,” Alice advises, as there is a knock on the front door.

“I’ll remember that,” Nicky says, putting down what he is doing and heading to the door, Alice walking behind him, and when get to the door Nicky opens it to reveal Lilia wearing a beautiful yellow robe. “Lilia, we told you didn’t have to knock,” Nicky reminds her as he greats her with a hug.

“It’s impolite not to,” Lilia responds, as she breaks apart from Nicky and walks over to Alice.

“Rio started a food fight last night and Agatha escalated it, I don’t think either of them care about being polite,” Alice reveal, though she has to admit it was fun.

“Of course they did,” Lilia says, not overly surprised as she hugs Alice. “Seems like you did a good job on the clean up,” Lilia says, walking into the living room, as she looks around and notices how clean the house appears as there is no signs that any kind of fight happened.

“We used magick, the clean-up was more fun than the fight,” Nicky reveals, though he did love seeing both his mothers so carefree.

“Of course you think that,” Lilia says amused. “And just where are your mothers?” Lilia asks Nicky as she realises, she doesn’t see either of them.

“Mama’s upstairs getting ready,” Nicky explains. “Mom is doing her job, but she swears she will be back in time,” Nicky explains.

“She’s cutting it close,” Lilia notes, taking notice of the time.

“I know, I said the same thing, but she promised she would be back in time,” Nicky admits, starting to feel nervous that she isn’t going to be.

“I don’t think we have anything to worry about,” Alice says, noticing the look on Nicky’s face. “Even Rio has enough self-preservation not to risk Agatha’s retribution by being late for this,” Alice admits, knowing that Rio missing the ceremony, even for her job, will be a disaster and that she wouldn’t want to be within a ten-mile radius of the conformation between Agatha and Rio that would result from that.

“Good to know,” Lilia says and as she does the doorbell rings.

“I’ll get it,” Agatha’s voice responds, and moments later she walks down the stairs wearing a dark purple princess style dress, with her hair down. Once she is at the foot of the stairs she walks over to the door and opens it to reveal Jen wearing pink dress similar to the one she wore on The Road. “Hi Jen,” Agatha greats.

“Wow, Agatha, you really couldn’t go with something a little more traditional?” Jen asks, taking notice of what Agatha is wearing, as she walks into the house, closing the door behind her.

“When have you ever known me to do something traditional?” Agatha asks.

“Good point,” Jen admits. “Still not overly sure why you’re doing this, you’re already married, in like multiple different ways,” Jen reminds Agatha as they walk towards the living area.

“True, but we’re not legally married, and we wanted to be legally married in front of all of you,” Agatha explains, as being able to be legally married is something she and Rio spent a long time not believing would ever be possible.

“Is it technically legal when neither of you actually exist?” Jen asks curious.

“Of course it is,” Agatha responds, starting to feel annoyed. “Can’t you just shut up and celebrate with us?” Agatha asks.

“I can celebrate, but I’m not going to shut up, and you wouldn’t want me to,” Jen says, knowing that, as while she and Agatha don’t hate each other anymore they have both realised that they like fighting and bickering with each other; just like real sisters.

“Okay, how about we save the bickering to later,” Nicky says, deciding it would be best to step in, and knowing from experience that there is no way his mama and Jen will stop bickering completely. “Please,” Nicky says, looking between Agatha and Jen.

“For you,” Jen says, and Agatha nods in agreement.

“Thank you,” Nicky says, looking relieved about that. “Mama, you look amazing,” Nicky says, walking over to her and hugging her, while Jen walks over to great Liila and Alice.

“While thank you, you don’t look to bad yourself,” Agatha tells her son, as she straightens his bowtie a little.

“Thank Mama,” Nicky says. “Now we just need Mom,” Nicky realises, and just as he says that the front door opens.

“I’m here, I’m here,” Rio says, running into the house and straight up the stairs. “I just need five minutes,” Rio says as she continues to run up the stairs.

“You heard her, five minutes,” Agatha tells the others. “You’ve got five minutes to get ready,” Agatha says, and as soon as she says that everyone else moves to where they know they are meant to be.

Exactly five minutes after Rio ran into the house Agatha is waiting in the living room when Rio, who is wearing a dark green buttoned up vest with matching pants, but no shirt, walks into the living room.

“You look incredible,” Agatha says, smiling at her.

“So do you,” Rio responds, walking straight over to Agatha “I really want to kiss you right now,” Rio admits, once she is right in front of Agatha.

“DON’T YOU DARE!” Nicky’s voice yells, causing both Agatha and Rio to laugh.

“We should probably get out there,” Agatha says, being pretty sure that if they don’t Nicky is going to come and get them as he is just as, maybe even more, excited about what is about to happen as they are.

“Yeah, we should,” Rio says, reaching out and taking Agatha’s hand.

Once they are holding each other’s hands Rio and Agatha head through the kitchen and into the backyard. As soon as they walk into the backyard, they find Nicky waiting for them, and a completely transformed backyard. From where Nicky is standing to an arch that is covered in flowers is an aisle, that is also made of flowers, and to the left of the aisle, a little way back from the arch, Jen is standing, while Alice is in the same position on the right side, and Lilia is standing directly in front of the arch.

“Mom,” Nicky says, offering his right arm to, and Rio links arms with him. “Mama,” Nicky says, doing the same with his left arm, and once he does that, he looks at Alice, who uses her magic to cause a harp to start softly playing.

As the music plays Nicky escorts his moms up the aisle and when they get to the end Nicky kisses both their cheeks, one at a time, before letting go and moving several steps back while his moms look at Liliia.

“It is my absolute pleasure to be here today, and I consider it an absolute privilege to be the one who you asked to complete this ceremony,” Lilia says as she looks between Agatha and Rio. “Two hundred and seventy-two years ago, when alone in a cleaning at midnight, you joined yourselves together magically, spiritual, by blood, and today you add legally to the list of ways you are already joined, with those who you are closest to here to bear witness,” Lilia says. “Over the centuries you have been together, and apart, felt hate and love, for one another, but you’ve always found your way back together, because that is the strength of your bond, of your connection, and today with your son and coven around you pledge yourselves to each other in another way, a way that was once considered impossible; even for us,” Lilia says. “Rio,” Lilia says, turning to her, and Rio turns to Agatha, taking both her hands.

“Agatha, I’ve spent an eternity watching humanity, watching people die because of love and hate, but it wasn’t until l met you that I understood why they would do that,” Rio admits. “Since the moment I first saw you, I knew you were special, but what I didn’t know is that you would become everything to me,” Rio admits. “I will be alive forever, but it is because of you, and our family, that I live; my heart truly beats for you, Agatha, I love you,” Rio says.

“Agatha,” Lilia says, smiling at her.

“Three hundred and thirty-three years ago after one of the worst moments of my life you can out of the shadows and turned it into one of the best,” Agatha says. “Suffering, hate, fear, prejudice, pain… that was all I knew, until you,” Agatha tells her. “Because of you I learnt to love, I learnt to feel good, and you’ve done everything you can to make me believe I deserve more than what I was given as a child,” Agatha says, fighting back her own emotion. “Rio, you may be death, but to me you’re life,” Agatha admits. “You saved me, loved me when I didn’t know what that was, and not only did you give me our son, but you also pulled off the impossible to bring him back to us. Even when was at my worse you believed I could be my best,” Agatha says. “You say your heart beats for me, well my soul is yours,” Agatha says. “Everything I am, is yours. You’re my love, my partner, my best friend, sometimes worse enemy, my everything; I love you; I trust you, I see you,” Agatha says to Rio.

“Rings,” Lilia says, and everyone turns to Nicky, who looks extremely nervous, as he really really doesn’t want to screw up what he is about to do.

“You’ve got it, Mi Conejito,” Rio tells him.

“Whatever you make we’re going to love,” Agatha assures him, as even after being together for so many years she and Rio have never had rings, and they both agreed that they whatever rings they got they wanted something that signifies not just them, but Nicky as well and because of that they asked him to create their rings.

“Okay, I can do this,” Nicky says, before muttering in lattin, and waving his right hand over his left, focusing on what he wants, and moments later, in a puff of blue magick two rings appear in his hand. While both rings are silver and have amethyst, sapphire and emerald stones, stones that clearly represent each of their magicks, how connected they are on the band, the layout of the stones are different. One of the rings has the amethyst in the middle with the sapphire and emerald either side, touching the slightly bigger amethyst, the other ring has the emerald in the middle. “Perfect,” Nicky says before offering the rings to his moms.

“Rio, do you take Agatha to be your lawful wedded wife?” Lilia asks, keeping it simple as she knows that the vows most people make in this situation don’t really apply.

“I do,” Rio says, taking the ring with the emerald in the middle from Nicky, before sliding the ring onto Agatha’s finger.

“Agatha, do you take Rio to be your lawful wedded wife?” Lilia asks.

“I do,” Agatha responds, as she takes the ring with the amethyst in the middle from Nicky before sliding it onto Rio’s finger.

“Then by the powers vested in me by the state of New Jersey, as well as the two of you, it is my pleasure to add legally married to the ways you already are, you may kiss each other,” Lilia says, and as soon as she says the words Agatha and Rio embrace, and kiss, each other, as their family, their coven, clap as Jen uses her magic to make small fireworks that can’t be seen by anyone outside the yard. After a few moments they finally break apart and Nicky hugs both his mothers, clearly thrilled for them.

Once they hug their son Rio and Agatha embrace the rest of their family, their coven, and spend the rest of the night celebrating, with those who matter most to them, their love that even after so many trials and tribulations continues to persevere.

The End
